Falkreath Barracks Exterior

**Falkreath Barracks** is the living quarters for the [Falkreath guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard") and also contains [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold")'s jail.

Falkreath's barracks

It is on the edge of Falkreath, southeast of the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)") and next door to [Grave Concoctions](/wiki/Skyrim:Grave_Concoctions "Skyrim:Grave Concoctions").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Falkreath Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard")  [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") (Prisoner) † |

**†** This person no longer resides here after starting the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight").

## Related Quests

- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.
- **[Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Help a guard overcome his skooma addiction.
- **[Once A Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Once_A_Hunter "Skyrim:Once A Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Elven_Hunter "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter"): Track down a hunter with a dangerous past.

### Exterior

At the rear of the building is a practice area where the guards can practice their melee and archery skills; there are two practice dummies and two archery targets. There is a flight of wooden stairs leading up to the balcony and the entrance to the sleeping quarters. There is also a well, three [thistle plants](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") and two [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") against the rock face, past the stairs, one of which is hidden behind the trees, and the other of which is further to the right, in line with the wooden fencing on the edge of the premise.

### Falkreath Barracks

The entrance leads to a room used by the [Falkreath guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard") to rest and relax in. It consists of a round wooden table and two chairs to the left and a flight of stairs up to the upper floor against the northeast wall. On the table are two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). Opposite the entrance is a flight of stairs leading down to the basement which is used as the jail. To the left of these stairs is a set of shelves holding four bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three of wine and three of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two pieces of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") and two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). There is a barrel of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") to the right with three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") on top and four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack above.

To the right of the stairs leading down to the jail is a square wooden table holding a copy of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, two [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") of differing strengths, three [potions of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") of differing strengths and a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"). The books *[Guard Dossier: Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dossier:_Aesrael "Skyrim:Guard Dossier: Aesrael")*, *[Guard's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Guard's Note")* and *[Guard's Bounty Letter Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Bounty_Letter_Draft "Skyrim:Guard's Bounty Letter Draft")* are also found on it. There is a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer") leaning against the wall to the left of the table. Against the southwest wall are several bales of straw with two practice dummies in front. To the right of the practice dummies there are two more food barrels with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") on top. There is a wooden bench against the northwest wall.

Upstairs is the dormitory with three single beds, two of which are owned, coming out from the southwest wall. They all have unlocked [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the beds and contain minor loot. A copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Legendary Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legendary_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:The Legendary Sancre Tor")* can be found on top of one of the chests. Against the southeast wall is a wooden bench with two bottles of Nord mead on the floor beside it. The northwest wall has a door that exits onto the balcony. To the right of the door is a round wooden table and two chairs. On the table are two bottles of alto wine and five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Above the stairs are two barrels with four bottles of Nord mead on top.

### Falkreath Jail

Falkreath's prison

Through the door into the jail is a room used by the guards. The main cell is opposite the entrance, against the southeast wall. Inside the adept-locked cell are two bedrolls, several sacks of foodstuffs in the far right corner of the cell and a table and chair on the northeastern wall holding two loaves of bread. Hidden behind the food sacks are several half loaves of bread and a lockpick. The guard's room has two wooden benches along the northwest wall. Against the southwest wall are several straw bales with a practice dummy in front and a pile of food sacks beside it. In the southern corner there are two food barrels, and to the left along the southeast wall are the prisoner belongings chest and the evidence chest. In the middle of the southern half of the room is a large wooden table and chair with one bottle of alto wine, one bottle of wine, and a copy of *[Rising Threat, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. III")* with a quill sitting next to it. To the left of the entrance are several crates and sacks, and tucked between the crates and the wall is a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")*. At the northeast end of the room is a partially partitioned area with crates, barrels, sacks, and a table and chair. On a barrel next to the southeast wall are copies of *[Rising Threat, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. I")* and *[II](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. II")*. At the end of the room is a separate cell used for [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding"). It looks like a well with knee-high water in the bottom, with spears blocking the entrance. Approaching the spears will cause Sinding to initiate conversation. If you agree to help him, the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight") will start and you will see him turn into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") and leap out the top of the well.

## Bugs

- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Falkreath, the new jailer here may be seen wearing [Stormcloak Officer Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Armor "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Armor") even though he isn't a Stormcloak officer. **?**

Falkreath Guard

**Falkreath Guards** are [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") who act as the military and police force of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). These guards serve under [Jarl Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"). Should the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") forces gain control of Falkreath, they will be replaced by [Stormcloak guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Guard "Skyrim:Stormcloak Guard") under the service of [Jarl Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn").

Falkreath guards are clad in a set of Falkreath guard's equipment. This includes a [Falkreath guard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard's Armor"), a [Falkreath guard's helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard's Helmet"), and a [Falkreath guard's shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard's Shield"). They also wear a pair of [fur boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Boots "Skyrim:Fur Boots"). They are equipped with an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and an [Imperial bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow") supplemented with 20 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"). They also carry a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a 50% chance of a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), and a variety of [leveled loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Pine forest in Falkreath

**Falkreath Hold** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in southern [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), with its capital in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It is initially affiliated with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), but can be captured by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") after completing [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad"). It can also change sides as part of negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

It is the second southernmost hold in Skyrim, after [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). It borders [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") in the south, across the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains"), and [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell") in the west. Other than its capital, Falkreath, the only notable town in the hold is [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), the first settlement in Skyrim to be attacked by a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").

Falkreath Hold is blanketed by characteristic pine forests and described by its citizens as being covered in a fine mist that makes it seem seasonless. The mountains rising above Falkreath are well above the snow line striking a stark comparison to the green of the rest of the hold. The most distinguishing geographic feature is [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta") which covers a large portion of the central region and acts as the source for the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River").

The town has the largest cemetery in Skyrim that houses generations of the dead, due to a large number of battles that have taken place over the years. The citizens take pride in this and many of the local shops and the farm derive their names from their close proximity to so much death.

Map of Falkreath Hold

Falkreath, the hold capital

## Flora and Fauna

The pine forest of Falkreath is very rich in [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), and all common varieties of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"). [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta") is home to a large population of different [fish species](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") which can be found near [the Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") and by the start of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). The hold is one of the few places where [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") is fairly common. In the snowy eastern parts only the [snowberry bush](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") thrives.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")** — A city in the south of Skyrim, and the capital of Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Angi's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Angi's Camp")** — A cabin and camp southeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angi%27s+Camp)
-  **[Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") west-southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anise%27s+Cabin)
- **[Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm")** — A small farmstead located in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Corpselight+Farm)
-  **[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary")** — An active [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dark+Brotherhood+Sanctuary)
-  **[Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill")** — A lumber mill that supplies [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Half-Moon+Mill)
-  **[Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen")** — A [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in eastern Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Helgen)
-  **[Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest")** — A small shack northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hunter%27s+Rest)
-  **[Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") — A piece of property in Falkreath Hold, north of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lakeview+Manor+%28HF%29)
-  **[Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch")** — A [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinewatch)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in Falkreath Hold, located east-northeast of [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven") and north of [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in Falkreath Hold, located east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
-  **[Secunda's Kiss](/wiki/Skyrim:Secunda%27s_Kiss "Skyrim:Secunda's Kiss")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") southwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Secunda%27s+Kiss)

### Caves

-  **[Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloated+Man%27s+Grotto)
-  **[Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bonechill+Passage)
-  **[Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") or [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Glenmoril+Coven)
-  **[Greywater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Greywater_Grotto "Skyrim:Greywater Grotto")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greywater+Grotto)
-  **[Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)
-  **[Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost"), and the powerful undead mage [Halldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir "Skyrim:Halldir"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halldir%27s+Cairn)
-  **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern")** — A small, open-roofed [cavernous](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") grove lush with many kinds of flora and fungi, located due north of [Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest") and northwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") which is inhabited by bears and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moss+Mother+Cavern)
-  **[South Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:South Brittleshin Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") and Falkreath Hold containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
-  **[Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing the conjurer [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") and his [coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)
-  **[Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sunderstone+Gorge)

### Dragon Lairs

-  **[Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent")** — A mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancient%27s+Ascent)

### Mines

-  **[Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine")** — A small [orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum "Skyrim:Orichalcum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bilegulch+Mine)
-  **[Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine")** — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Embershard+Mine)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic Ruins

-  **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleak+Falls+Barrow)
-  **[North Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:North Shriekwind Bastion")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shriekwind+Bastion)
-  **[Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Roadside+Ruins)
-  **[South Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:South Shriekwind Bastion")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shriekwind+Bastion)
-  **[Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher")** — The location of the Pilgrim's Path and main entrance to [Nocturnal's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal") Ebonmere portal, resting place for the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Twilight+Sepulcher)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Bannermist Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Bannermist_Tower "Skyrim:Bannermist Tower")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bannermist+Tower)
-  **[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle"), and [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodlet+Throne)
-  **[Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Hunter "Skyrim:Orc Hunter") led by [Ghunzul](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghunzul "Skyrim:Ghunzul"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cracked+Tusk+Keep)
-  **[Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower")** — A small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Watchtower)
-  **[Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Neugrad)
-  **[Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)
- **[North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch")** — A small [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") and [ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
-  **[Peak's Shade Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Peak%27s_Shade_Tower "Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Peak%27s+Shade+Tower)
- **[South Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:South Skybound Watch")** — A small [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") and [ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

The Guardian Stones

-  **[The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones")** — A location which marks three [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") located directly outside of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Guardian+Stones)
  -  **[The Mage Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mage_Stone "Skyrim:The Mage Stone")** [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Guardian+Stones)
  -  **[The Thief Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Thief_Stone "Skyrim:The Thief Stone")** [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Guardian+Stones)
  -  **[The Warrior Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrior_Stone "Skyrim:The Warrior Stone")** [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Guardian+Stones)
-  **[The Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Lady+Stone)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small glade in a cavern east-southeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ancestor+Glade+%28DG%29)
-  **[Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove")** — A grove of trees concealing a small pond fed by a rocky stream, just southwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Evergreen+Grove)
- **[Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the southern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jerall+Mountains)
- **[Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta")** — A lake in west-central Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Ilinalta)
-  **[Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock")** — A wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") led by a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)
- **[White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River")** — The longest river in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"), stretching from the south of the province to the northeast corner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River)

### Unmarked Places

- There are three [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in Falkreath Hold.
  - North of [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine").
  - South of [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove").
  - West of [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").
- There are a few [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in Falkreath Hold.
  - A [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") south of [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones").
  - A [Shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") northeast of [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher").
  - Two [Shrines of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") outside Falkreath's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)").
- The [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds a ritual site north of [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").

Bandit Bridge: Pinewatch

- Unmarked Bandit Camps
  - South of [The Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones") there is a camp inhabited by three bandits. The camp has three tents with a bedroll each, one [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a tanning rack. One of the bandits carries *[Treasure Map I](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_I "Skyrim:Treasure Map I")*. There is a coin purse and a satchel resting on a tree stump. A copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[Night Falls on Sentinel](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Falls_on_Sentinel "Skyrim:Night Falls on Sentinel")* can be found in one of the tents. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=3195&y=-66333&zoom=17&legacy=true)
  - West of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") is a camp consisting of a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"), a chest, a potion of healing, a pair of hide boots, three bedrolls and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")*. One [beehive](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive "Skyrim:Beehive") in a tree north of the campfire. Even if you just try to lockpick a chest, two archers and one melee bandit will appear from the west. Further attempts won't spawn anyone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=4240&y=-78883&zoom=17&legacy=true)
  - Southwest of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). It consists of two towers that straddle the [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen")-[Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") road, linked by a rope bridge. A bandit archer keeps watch atop each tower. A tripwire activates a [boulder trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") that is attached to the structure. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-13280&y=-80576&zoom=17&legacy=true)
  - South of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") is a camp on the base of a waterfall inhabited by two melee [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and one mage ([Expert difficulty](/wiki/Skyrim:Difficulty "Skyrim:Difficulty")). A copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Lunar Lorkhan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lunar_Lorkhan "Skyrim:The Lunar Lorkhan")* can be found inside a tent, and there is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") just outside. Next to the tent lies a dead [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)") on a fallen tree, as well as an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-6428&y=-85559&zoom=17&legacy=true)

## Falkreath Hold Quests

All quests that are started in or are related to Falkreath Hold (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad")**: Rescue [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldiers from the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and capture the [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.
- **[A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").
- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.
- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

### Bards College

- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").

### Dark Brotherhood

- All the Dark Brotherhood primary quests except for [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!"), and most of the other quests received before Hail Sithis!, are related to Falkreath Hold.

### Thieves Guild

- **[Darkness Returns](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkness_Returns "Skyrim:Darkness Returns")**: Walk the [Pilgrim's Path](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher") and return the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key") to its rightful place.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Companions

- **[Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor")**: Claim the head of a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") for [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").

### Side Quests including Divine Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").
- **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)")**: Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.

### Creation Club Quests

- **[The Dwarven Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Crown "Skyrim:The Dwarven Crown")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Gather all the components of a powerful Dwarven Crown from within a [forgotten Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Runoff_Caverns "Skyrim:Runoff Caverns").
- **[The Dwarven Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dwarven_Horse "Skyrim:The Dwarven Horse")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Reassemble an ancient Dwarven [vamidium](/wiki/Lore:Vamidium "Lore:Vamidium").
- **[Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons"): Shut down a malfunctioning Dwarven weather machine.
- **[Once A Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Once_A_Hunter "Skyrim:Once A Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Elven_Hunter "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter"): Track down a hunter with a dangerous past.
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.
- **[The Rising Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rising_Dead "Skyrim:The Rising Dead")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead"): A group of [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") plan to summon an army of [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie").

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests are located in Falkreath Hold. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

# Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp

## Overview

Falkreath Imperial Camp

**Falkreath Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), located east-northeast of [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven") and north of [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge").

Falkreath Imperial Camp

This camp will only be present if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") hold [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") and the rest of Falkreath Hold, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Legate Skulnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Skulnar "Skyrim:Legate Skulnar"), except during the related quest, when [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") takes command. Like similar Imperial camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has neither a [quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster") or any [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). Unlike most military camps, it also has no [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Skulnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Skulnar "Skyrim:Legate Skulnar") (commander)  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad")**: Retake [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

## Falkreath Imperial Camp

It is a typical Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. There is an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside the fire. To the west of the campfire is the command tent, containing a round table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. South of the campfire is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. To the right of this tent is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). To the southeast is the hospital tent, containing three bed rolls, two of which are occupied by wounded soldiers, and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the left is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). Northeast of the campfire is a row of three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. To the right of the first of these tents is an owned [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"). There are many [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") in and around the camp.

Any time [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents.

## Notes

- Two ore veins are near the camp: a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein north of the camp, and an [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein northeast of the camp.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

Falkreath Stormcloak Camp

**Falkreath Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), located east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").

Falkreath Stormcloak Camp

The camp is normally commanded by [Thorygg Sun-Killer](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorygg_Sun-Killer "Skyrim:Thorygg Sun-Killer"), except during the related quest, at which point [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will assume command. The camp is initially disabled, and is only enabled after you are sent to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") during [Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm"), or you complete either [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks") or Joining the Legion.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Thorygg Sun-Killer](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorygg_Sun-Killer "Skyrim:Thorygg Sun-Killer") (commander)  [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster")  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad")**: Rescue [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldiers from the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and capture the [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Falkreath Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [charred skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") cooking over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Around the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. Northeast of the campfire is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, an end table, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. To the southeast are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. South of the campfire is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), while to the north is the hospital tent, which contains four hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers. Outside the hospital tent is a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), next to another table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). Northeast of the hospital tent is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. Between the hospital tent and the campfire is the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table holds various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). To the left of the workbench are some barrels.

Any time [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- When the camp is enabled for the first time it permanently disables an unmarked place of a [Khajiit Caravan Massacre](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Falkreath#Khajiit_Caravan_Massacre "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Falkreath") south-southwest with a skill book [The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game").
- East of the camp is a den guarding by two wolfs with human and animal skeletal remains and a coin purse among them, when Falkreath Stormcloak Camp is enabled for the first time it permanently disables a Nord's corpse carrying a skill book [Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale"). Behind the cave, up the hill farther east, is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein").
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

## Bugs

- The [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster") is enabled before the camp is enabled **?**

# Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Imperial Tower.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Imperial_Tower.png) | Imperial Tower: Falkreath Watchtower ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Watchtower)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Falkreath_Watchtower "Lore:Falkreath Watchtower")) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |

Falkreath Watchtower

**Falkreath Watchtower** is a small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer").

## Related Quests

- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Camp atop the tower

The tower is at the end of a dirt path heading south from the road along the southern shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"); the path is marked by a pile of rocks west of the junction with the road to Falkreath. Several [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") grow along the edge of the path, which curves east to approach the tower. The grim trophy of a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") on the left side of the path speaks to the depravity ahead. Just past the spriggan's remains, to the northwest is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). A flight of stone steps leads up to the arched tower entrance.

On the ground floor is a toppled set of shelves holding [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and gory human remains. To the right of the shelves are more gory remains on a stake beside curved stone stairs leading up. The only other items on this level are three barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks. The stairs lead to the top of the tower, where you'll find a leveled necromancer. There is also the corpse of a female [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_(dead) "Skyrim:Khajiit (dead)"), whom the necromancer will raise to assist in fighting you. She is not armed, however, so you can safely ignore her and concentrate on the necromancer. One way to deal with the necromancer is to keep moving forward while attacking, forcing them to retreat until they fall from the tower to their death.

A central campfire features a soul gem stand holding an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). Near the ruined wall is the necromancer's small tent containing a bedroll, a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Liminal Bridges](/wiki/Skyrim:Liminal_Bridges "Skyrim:Liminal Bridges")*, and a copy of *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*. The only other item of interest is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") next to the tent.

## Notes

- The location data for this cell refers to it as "Crossroads Watchtower". This causes the location to be referenced in the quest journal as such, as the journal pulls directly from the location data.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. The location is now referenced in the location data as "Falkreath Watchtower", consistent with the map marker.

Falkreath Watchtower

**Falkreath Watchtower** is a small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The tower is at the end of a dirt path heading south from the road along the southern shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"); the path is marked by a pile of rocks west of the junction with the road to Falkreath. Falkreath

**Falkreath** is a city in the south of Skyrim, and the capital of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). It is initially aligned with the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") under [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"). Near the borders with [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") and [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell"), in the past it was considered a part of Cyrodiil, but now sits firmly within the borders of Skyrim. Falkreath's economy is centered around lumber retrieved from the surrounding forest. Falkreath's most distinguishing feature is its large cemetery housing generations of dead from throughout Skyrim; the cemetery is also an important cultural landmark for the residents of Falkreath, directly inspiring the names of several businesses and homes within the city.

For more information on Falkreath, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Falkreath "Lore:Falkreath").

#### Daedric

- **[A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").
- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

#### Creation Club

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.
- **[Once A Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Once_A_Hunter "Skyrim:Once A Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Elven_Hunter "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter"): Track down a hunter with a dangerous past.

([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Return to Dengeir | [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") or [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") |

#### Creation Club

- **[Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Help a guard overcome his skooma addiction.

## Notes

- With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, you can purchase [a plot of land](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor") in Falkreath Hold to build a house on. Also, three [stone quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone") will be present, and you can use the grain mill to make [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour").
- Almost all of the town's residents have an odd internal quirk. With the exception of Delacourt, Rayya, Sinding, Skulnar, Valdr, and the Dark Brotherhood members, every NPC possesses two versions of almost all of their greetings. In many cases, these are different versions of the same greeting performed by the respective voice actors (this is the case for Helvard, Indara, Lod, Mathies, Narri, Nenya, Siddgeir, Solaf, Valga, and Zaria), while others seem to have only one voice take for a line of dialogue duplicated with two different filenames (this is the case for Bolund, Kust, Runil, Tekla, and Thadgeir). Dengeir is a unique case: most of his duplicate lines are identical, with the exception of a single line that also has a different subtitle. This quirk is otherwise only seen with the unused NPC [Mithorpa Nasyal](/wiki/Skyrim:Mithorpa_Nasyal "Skyrim:Mithorpa Nasyal"). Regardless, due to one version of each greeting being ordered above the other, only one can ever be heard in the game, leaving the other unused.
- Despite going unnamed in the final game as it has no interiors or map markers, the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* refers to the local mill as **Deadwood Lumber Mill**, befitting the town's specific naming convention.
- Falkreath appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Falcrenth](/wiki/Arena:Falcrenth "Arena:Falcrenth"), [ESO](/wiki/Online:Falkreath_Hold "Online:Falkreath Hold") and *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Falkreath "Legends:Falkreath")*.

# Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Fallowstone Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fallowstone+Cave)) | | |

Fallowstone Cave

**Fallowstone Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). It contains only one zone, *[Fallowstone Cave](#Fallowstone_Cave)*.

Before starting the quest [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe"), the tunnel in the cave leading to the exit to [Giant's Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Grove "Skyrim:Giant's Grove") will be blocked.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Before progressing the quest The Cursed Tribe, many blood splatters and bones, including a mammoth rib cage, litter the area along the approach and around the entrance. A few [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") grow around the entrance. When you arrive during the quest, several of the larger rocks around the entrance will be painted with designs typical of giants, while [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") will be hanging from the overhang by the entrance.

### Fallowstone Cave

Cave interior

**If you are not here during the quest The Cursed Tribe:** When you first enter, there is a tunnel heading east before turning to the south and opening into a massive high-roofed cavern. In front of you is a large stream formed by a waterfall to the west, which then falls in two steps to the very bottom of the cavern. There is another waterfall to the east that joins the stream after the first drop, forming a powerful surge by the time it reaches the lowest level. As you emerge from the entrance tunnel, there are a couple of piles of rock near a mammoth rib cage. There are two leveled animals or other creatures (which may include [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") or [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll")) and a frostbite spider nearby, one on either side of the stream. Behind the ribs is an earthen bridge that crosses the stream. Several rock pillars support the ceiling throughout the cavern, with vegetation obscuring some of the fungi and flora listed below. Descending one level to the east, you will see a small tunnel ahead, which contains another frostbite spider and a [dead Orc bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Orc_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)").

**If you are here during the quest The Cursed Tribe:** Giants will have moved in, killing a large number of the animals and adding several large painted rocks and strings of bones. There is also a dead Orc leaning against one of the large rocks next to the first mammoth rib cage, with blood splattered on the ground nearby. The way forward lies across the earthen bridge to the southeast. There are several descending "steps" formed by ledges, which allow for drops sufficiently short to avoid damage. Continue heading southeast, and after a few drops, you will find a tunnel opening in the east wall to the south surrounded by cobwebs. The tunnel only extends a few paces before it comes to a dead end, with a dead Orc bandit, a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

Head northeast from here until you reach one of the last ledges, where you can see the bottom of the cavern and across the far side of the stream. There are more leveled animals in this area, although some may already be dead if they have fought each other. As you reach the stream, you will find it splits, with one fork flowing southwest to northeast, and the other flowing west to east. Crossing the stream, but keeping the first fork on your right, there are two [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") next to each other against the west wall of the cavern. Following the cavern wall around, there is a section featuring several trees naturally lit by a hole in the ceiling. Farther to the southeast against the cavern wall is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"), with a tunnel carved by the stream farther to the right. During the quest, a small camp with a single giant will be found just north of the iron ore vein. The camp will include a large fire in the middle, and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), and a random healing potion next to a cart beside the fire.

Following the stream down the tunnel leads to another cave, where the stream broadens and flows straight across the cave before disappearing underground near the exit to the southeast. During the quest, a giant will be standing near a small flooded alcove by the northeast wall; the alcove contains a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and a random potion. If you're not here during the quest, there are two more leveled animals at this point, with two more not far away that may be alerted to any fighting, and only the random potion will be found in the alcove. Opposite, the cave rises to the southwest wall, which has another small alcove. This alcove is dry, and contains a [dead Orc bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#EncBandit01Melee1HOrcM "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") next to a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Effects "Skyrim:Enchanting Effects") [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons").

The exit passage is to the southeast, and rises sharply as it turns to the southwest and then to the northwest. During the quest, two bone chimes will be hanging from the ceiling at the entrance to this tunnel, but they are too high for you to trigger accidentally. At the top, the passage opens into a small cave containing an apprentice-locked chest and two leveled animals, unless they came to investigate fighting earlier. The cave is covered in bones, both humanoid and animal, and features the body of an Orc. Just past the corpse is a tunnel rising to the southwest, which leads to the exit to Giant's Grove.

North of the exit passage is the entrance to a narrow tunnel, which also rises quite steeply to the northwest. This tunnel leads back into the massive main cavern, onto a narrow ledge that follows the wall of the cavern to the west. Continue following the ledge until you have passed a mammoth skull, after which it is safe to drop off the edge to land on the top ledge where you initially entered the cave.

## Notes

- You cannot wait in the cave.
- The cave contains the following harvestable ingredients: 2 [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), 7 [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 4 [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), 1 [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 1 [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), 1 [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), 1 [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), and 5 [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap").
- Northwest of the cave, under a tree north of the road near the mountains, is a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")*. A short distance to the northwest is a silver ore vein and an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein").
- A [Fallowstone Hall](/wiki/Online:Fallowstone_Hall "Online:Fallowstone Hall") appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"), although it bears no apparent relation to Fallowstone Cave and is in a different location.

Falmer Servant

**Falmer Servants** are hostile servants of the twisted [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and can be found throughout [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach").

They all wear [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") and their weapons are randomly determined between a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), all of them leveled up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 23. They also carry a leveled amount of gold and may carry one or two alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

They will attack you if there are any Falmer nearby. They will warn you off but not attack if you keep your distance, so long as no Falmer are nearby. These servants are not hostile to any type of Falmer and the Falmer are not hostile to them.

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") at [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr").
2. Travel to the randomly-determined location
3. Retrieve the heirloom from the location's boss chest.
4. Return the heirloom to Skjor or Vilkas for your reward.

### The Family Heirloom

When you tell Skjor (or Vilkas) you are looking for work, he will say: *"We have a bit of a sensitive matter this time. A wealthy family has... misplaced one of their heirlooms."* or *"Just in time. I was worried I'd have to do this myself. Some rich folk had a trinket stolen and they want us to get it back."* He will then provide some information on the kind of place you need to go and what you are up against:

| Enemy Type | Job Description |
| --- | --- |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | *"I tell you this province is losing its grip. The bandits become more brazen every day."* |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") | *"Some don't even believe they exist, but the Falmer can be devious. Tunneling into homes, stealing off with valuables."* |
| [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") | *"Those hill people who call themselves 'the Forsworn' show no mercy."* |
| [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") | *"Giants don't usually cause problems like this, but these ones are stirred up for some reason.."* |
| [Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") | *"The rumors say the culprits are vampires. I try not to listen to swaggle like that, but figured you should know."* |
| [Warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") | *"Of course, it's a group of wizards they're pointing their fingers at. Who knows what they want it for, but we want it back."* |

### The Location

The stolen item is randomly determined, from a list that includes all standard unenchanted [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") in the game. You are never told the name of the family who lost the item, only the hold in which they live.

A [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowpoint_Beacon "Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon") inhabited by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit")

The target location is randomly chosen from 76 possible locations, amounting to a large fraction of the [dungeons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") that contain boss chests. The location will be limited to holds that you have previously visited, so early in the game you may only receive destinations within Whiterun Hold, but later in the game there are many more possible destinations. Possible types of locations are:

- A [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") Camp or Bandit-Occupied Fort: 23 possible locations ([Bandit Camps category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps"))
- A [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") Hive: 12 possible locations ([Falmer Hives category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer_Hives "Category:Skyrim-Places-Falmer Hives"))
- A [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") Camp: 7 possible locations ([Forsworn Camps category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Forsworn Camps"))
- A [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") Camp: 12 possible locations ([Giant Camps category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Giant_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Giant Camps"))
- A [Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") Lair: 8 possible locations ([Vampire Lairs category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Vampire Lairs"))
- A [Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") Lair: 15 possible locations ([Warlock Lairs category](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"))

(Note that the provided categories list all locations with the given type of occupant, including locations that do *not* have a boss chest and therefore cannot be possible destinations for this quest).

### Find the Heirloom

At the chosen location, the item will always be found in the boss chest, which is typically at the end of the dungeon and guarded by a boss-level monster. To complete the quest, all that you need to do is retrieve the item — although in the process of exploring the dungeon you may end up collecting other loot and killing various enemies. Once you have the heirloom, return to the quest-giver (Skjor or Vilkas) and obtain your reward and three different responses: *"Give it here. They've asked for the utmost discretion on this matter, so I'll make sure it gets to them. Here's your share of their reward."*, *"And it looks undamaged. They'll be pleased, I'm sure. And we're pleased with their money."* or *"Nice work with this one. You make us all proud."*

### Reward

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- The quest-giver for this quest is originally [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor"). However, once Skjor has been slain during [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") instead becomes the quest giver for this quest.
- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).

## Bugs

- The item you are sent to retrieve may not spawn at the location indicated by your quest map marker.
- The quest may get broken, showing in the questlog like "Retrieve [...] from [...]", and with the quest map marker indicating one of the hidden NPC chests beneath the surface of the game.

## Quest Stages

| Family Heirloom (CR06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | A family in <Alias=LocationHold> had a valuable stolen. They believe the culprits took it to <Alias=Location>, and I'm to retrieve it for them. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the <Alias=Gewgaw> from <Alias=Location> |
| 20 |  | I recovered a stolen <Alias=Gewgaw> from <Alias=Location> for a noble family in <Alias=LocationHold>. *Objective 20:* Return to <Alias=Questgiver> |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR06`.
