Farkas

**Farkas** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") and member of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"). While, as his twin brother [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") puts it, *"his brains are not his strong suit"*, Farkas is respected as a skilled warrior.

He and Vilkas belong to the Companions' [inner circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") and, as such, are both [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").

Farkas appears morally ambivalent about being a werewolf, and is hesitant to use his [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form"). He can be loose with his tongue, often showing impertinence to his elders. However, he warms up quickly to you when met, and is quick to protect his friends.

He wears a random set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor") and is armed with a [Skyforge steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Greatsword") (or an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") at lower levels). He also carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and the [key to the Whiterun gate](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Gate_Key "Skyrim:Whiterun Gate Key").

He offers both miscellaneous quests and master level [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"). During the [journey to Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), Farkas will refuse to accompany you past the outer chambers, admitting that he has developed a fear of giant spiders following your initiation trial in the quest [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor").

#### Companions Quests

- **[Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
- **[Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor")**: Claim a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with Farkas or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon.
- **[Hired Muscle](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Muscle "Skyrim:Hired Muscle")**: Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to bring a citizen back in line.
- **[Purity](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity")**: Help a member of the Circle give up their beasthood.
- **[Trouble in Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Trouble_in_Skyrim "Skyrim:Trouble in Skyrim")**: Fulfill a contract for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a troublesome area.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

When first meeting him outside [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm"):

:   *"You look strong. Come to Jorrvaskr and be a Companion!"*

When approaching him:

:   *"My brother Vilkas is a better talker than me. He should be around someplace."*

:   **Who are the Companions?**
:   *"The Companions are my family. We fight so that other people don't have to. We bring honor and glory to ourselves and each other."*

:   **Why did you join the Companions?**
:   *"Vilkas and I have been here since we were little whelps. Our father, Jergen, raised us here. Even Vignar couldn't remember Companions younger than us!"*

:   **What does it mean to be a Companion?**
:   *"I've never been a smart one. But the Companions welcome anyone with the heart of a warrior. When we step into battle, we fight for our own name, and the name of the Companions."*

:   **Where do you stand on the war?**
:   *"Too confusing for me. Empire, Nords, Talos. Who cares? Just tell me who needs bludgeoning."*

:   **Can I join the Companions?**
:   *"Kodlak is the one who figures out who can be a Companion. So talk to him. It's out of my hands."*

Asking his opinion on being a werewolf after becoming [initiated](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") within the ranks of the Circle, he will answer the following:

:   **What's it like being a werewolf?**
:   *"I like being stronger when I become the wolf. But [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") says it is bad for the soul, and I trust him."*

His greetings can be:

:   *"Skjor says I have the strength of Ysgramor, and my brother has his smarts."*
:   *"Some people don't think I'm smart. Those people get my fist. But you, I like."*
:   *"Getting tired of hanging around talking all day."*
:   *"Thinking I need to train some more."*
:   *"I'm here to help."*
:   *"For Kodlak!"* **(During Glory of the Dead)**
:   *"Vilkas says you're the new Kodlak. I don't know what that means, but you seem honorable, so that's good."* **(After Glory of the Dead)**
:   *"Oh, you don't need to worry about me. I do what I'm told. Congratulations!"* **(After becoming the new Harbinger)**

### Take Up Arms

After bringing [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") her shield, she states the following:

:   *"Here, let's have Farkas show you where you'll be resting your head."*

[Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") will call for Farkas, who appears rushing into the room. His dialogue depends on whether or not you met the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") at [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm").

:   **Skjor:** *"Farkas!"*
:   **Farkas:** *"Did you call me?"*
:   **Aela:** *"Of course we did, icebrain. Show this new blood where the rest of the whelps sleep."*
:   **Farkas:** *"New blood? Oh, I remember you. Come on, follow me." OR "New blood? Oh, hello. I'm Farkas. Come on, follow me."*

Farkas will then walk you to your quarters, all the while giving some background information:

:   *"Skjor and Aela like to tease me, but they're good people. They challenge us to be our best."*
:   *"Nice to have a new face around. It gets boring here sometimes. I hope we keep you. This can be a rough life."*
:   *"The quarters are up here. Just pick a bed and fall in it when you're tired. Tilma will keep the place clean. She always has."*

Once arriving at the whelps' quarters:

:   *"All right, so here you are. Looks like the others are eager to meet you. Come to me or Aela if you're looking for work. Once you've made a bit of a name for yourself, Skjor and Vilkas might have things for you to do. Good luck. Welcome to the Companions."*

Which he will follow up by saying:

:   *"By the way, if you're looking for something to do..."*

This ends Take Up Arms, and Farkas will offer you one of his radiant quests.

### Proving Honor

Approaching Farkas inside Jorrvaskr will lead to him to informing you that Skjor was looking for you.

:   *"Skjor was looking for you, earlier."*
:   **What does he want?**
:   *"Don't know. He just said he needed to talk to you before you do anything else. I don't like making him angry, but there is some work for you if you want it."*

Skjor assigns you a mission to retrieve a [fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), with Farkas acting as your Shield-Brother and observer. He will explain this will be the final test for Companion membership. After the conversation, you will be directed to Farkas:

:   *"I hope you've readied yourself."*
:   **You're going to be my Shield-Brother?**
:   *"So I'm told. Let's see if you impress."*

Farkas will become your follower, dismissing any of your previous followers. Speaking to him allows for additional dialogue:

:   **Who was this scholar?**
:   *"A smart man came and told us about a blade piece. Skjor thinks you should find it, and I'm supposed to watch you."*

:   **Why did Skjor call this my Trial?**
:   *"I watch you to make sure you are honorable. If you are honorable and strong, then I can call you brother/sister."*

:   **What is Wuuthrad?**
:   *"Ysgramor was the hero who started the Companions. Wuuthrad was his weapon. He came from the ancient homeland and killed all the elves. But not all of them, because some of them are still here."*

:   **I'll meet you at Dustman's Cairn**
:   *"Don't delay, Shield-Brother/Sister."*

Once entering Dustman's Cairn:

:   *"Looks like someone's been digging here, and recently. Tread lightly."*
:   *"Be careful around the burial stones. I don't want to haul you back to Jorrvaskr on my back."*

At a certain point, you will trap yourself behind a gate and trigger a scene:

:   *"Now look what you've gotten yourself into. No worries, just sit tight. I'll find a release."*
:   *"What was that?"*

At this point, five [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") members enter the room.

:   **Silver Hand Member:** *"Killing you will make for an excellent story."*
:   **Farkas:** *"None of you will be alive to tell it."*

Farkas will then transform into a werewolf, kill all the Silver Hand members, and open the gate. Once back in his human form he will speak to you once more:

:   *"I hope I didn't scare you."* After killing all Silver Hand members, opening the gate, and returning in human form.

:   **What was that?**
:   *"It's a blessing given to some of us. We can be like wild beasts. Fearsome."*

:   **You're going to make me a werewolf?**
:   *"Oh, no. Only the Circle have the beastblood. Prove your honor to be a Companion. "Eyes on the prey, not the horizon." We should keep moving. Still the draugr to worry about."*

When speaking to Farkas after the encounter:

:   *"We should keep moving."*

:   **The Companions are werewolves?**
:   *"Not everyone, but all in the Circle are. It's a secret to everybody."*

:   **Who are the Silver Hand?**
:   *"Bad people who don't like werewolves. So they don't like us either."*

After obtaining the Wuuthrad Fragment:

:   *"We need to get back to Jorrvaskr."*

Once you have recovered the fragment of Wuuthrad from Dustman's Cairn and returned to Jorrvaskr, Vilkas will tell you to stand before the Circle for judgement. Harbinger [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") will then start off:

:   **Kodlak:** *"Brothers and Sisters of the Circle, today we welcome a new soul into our mortal fold. This man/woman has endured, has challenged and has showed his/her valor. Who will speak for him/her?"*
:   **Farkas:** *"I stand witness for the courage of the soul before us."*
:   **Kodlak:** *"Would you raise your shield in his/her defense?"*
:   **Farkas:** *"I would stand at his/her back, that the world might never overtake us."*
:   **Kodlak:** *"And would you raise your sword in his/her honor?"*
:   **Farkas:** *"It stands ready to meet the blood of his/her foes."*
:   **Kodlak:** *"And would you raise a mug in his/her name?"*
:   **Farkas:** *"I would lead the song of triumph as our mead hall reveled in his/her stories."*
:   **Kodlak:** *"Then this judgment of this Circle is complete. His/her heart beats with fury and courage that have united the Companions since the days of the distant green summers. Let it beat with ours, so the mountains may echo and our enemies may tremble at the call."*
:   **Everyone:** *"It shall be so."*

### Kodlak's Funeral

Farkas will be present at Kodlak's Funeral, and contribute to a speech held by Eorlund and the remaining Circle members.

:   **Eorlund:** *"Who will start?"*
:   **Aela:** *"I'll do it. Before the ancient flame... We grieve."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"We grieve."*
:   **Farkas:** *"We grieve."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"We grieve."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"At this loss... We weep."*
:   **Aela:** *"We weep."*
:   **Farkas:** *"We weep."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"We weep."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"For the fallen... We shout."*
:   **Aela:** *"We shout."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"We shout."*
:   **Farkas:** *"We shout."*
:   **Farkas:** *"And for ourselves... We take our leave."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"We take our leave."*
:   **Aela:** *"We take our leave."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"We take our leave."*
:   **Aela:** *"His spirit is departed. Members of the Circle, let us withdraw to the Underforge, to grieve our last together."*

### Glory of the Dead

Starting off this quest, the remaining Circle members have a discussion in the [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge") about Kodlak's final wishes. Farkas speaks only speaks once during this debate, adding that:

:   "Kodlak did not care for vengeance."

The Circle eventually agrees to head to [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb") to cure Kodlak's lycanthropy so he can ascend to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)"). Arriving at the tomb and progressing through, Farkas will withdraw from the fight once reaching a spider den, stating the following:

:   *"I can't go any further, Shield-Brother/Sister."*
:   **What's the matter?**
:   *"Ever since Dustman's Cairn, the big crawly ones have been too much for me. Everyone has his weakness, and this one is mine. I'm not proud, but I will stay back with Vilkas. Give my regards to Ysgramor."*

He then leaves you and Aela to finish the quest.

### Purity

After Glory of the Dead, you can speak to him again for more radiant quests. Eventually, he will voice his distain of being a werewolf, offering the quest [Purity](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity").

:   **Is there any work to be done?**
:   *"Of course, there is always work. My mind is someplace else, though."*

:   :   **What troubles you?**
    :   *"I think that maybe Kodlak was right. As a werewolf, I can't be a good Nord. I want to be clean, like he was, and go to Sovngarde when I finally die."*

:   :   :   **I will help you cure yourself.**
        :   *"I would be honored for you to accompany me, Harbinger."*

:   :   :   **This is a personal matter, and I leave it to you.**
        :   *"Thank you, Harbinger."* **(Declining the quest)**

:   *"Aela said we would need a Hagraven's head. I already have one of them, but she said it was a special kind. And that you knew where to get more. Let's go find one!"* **(If you don't have a Glenmoril Witch head.)**
:   *"You still have one of the witch's heads. This is good. Let's go to the Tomb. We can do the cleansing there."* **(If you have a Glenmoril Witch head.)**

After obtaining a Glenmoril Witch head, Farkas can be spoken to:

:   *"Did you take the head?"*
:   **I have it.**
:   *"This is good. Could you show the way to the tomb again?"*

After clearing Ysgramor's Tomb and defeating Farkas' wolf spirit:

:   *"Is it over?"*
:   **Are you ok?** **or** **Get up. Did it work?**
:   *"It's like relaxing into a warm mug of spiced mead. I'm losing aches I didn't know I had. This is how a warrior should feel. Alive and aware. Not clouded with thoughts of the hunt. Thank you for your help. I'm going to stay in the tomb for a while. My shame kept me out before, but now I want to see it."*

### Dragon Seekers

Speaking to Farkas for radiant quests leads to him voicing his interest in slaying a dragon and offering the quest [Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers"), even if he has encountered one prior to the quest.

:   **Is there any work to be done?**
:   *"Travelers have been coming to Whiterun. They tell stories about dragons. I've heard of them, but didn't think they were real. Have you ever seen one?"*

:   :   **Yes, they're real. I've seen them.**
    :   *"You are a very brave man/woman. But I already knew that."*

:   :   **Maybe one day you'll see one yourself.**
    :   *"Not at this rate. I'll just go back to clubbing horkers and scaring the debtors."*

:   :   **Rumors and ramblings should be ignored.**
    :   *"That is the kind of thing Kodlak used to say. And he was right. But still, I'd like to see for myself."*

:   **Let's go kill a dragon.**
:   *"Well, that's one way to find out if they're real. I even know where we might find one. Lead on!"*

After defeating the dragon:

:   *"Now that was a battle!"*

:   :   **You fought well.**
    :   *"Thank you, Harbinger."*

:   :   **Next time, try harder.**
    :   *"I will train better for the future."*

:   :   **Let's go.**
    :   *"You go if you want to. I've never seen bones this large, and want to make sure I remember them so I can tell the story right. Otherwise Vilkas will just say I was making it up."*

:   *"We bring honor to the Companions."*

## Conversations

Various conversations held between Farkas and other members of the Companions can be overheard.

:   **Athis**: *"You might do well to learn a new weapon. Vary your style a bit."*
:   **Farkas**: *"Tiny blades don't hurt enough. A sword needs weight."*
:   **Athis**: *"But ten little cuts..."*
:   **Farkas**: *"All I need is one to cut you in half."*
:   **Athis**: *"Well, when you put it that way..."*

:   **Farkas**: *"You only use the little swords."*
:   **Athis**: *"It's called a shortsword, oaf. It's quicker. Sharper. Like a razorfish against a [whale](/wiki/Lore:Whale "Lore:Whale")."*
:   **Farkas**: *"But whales eat razorfish."*
:   **Athis**: *"And they always come to regret it."*

:   **Farkas**: *"Relax, new blood."*
:   **Torvar**: *"I've been hunting on my own for years."*
:   **Farkas**: *"Fighting people is different. Smarter."*
:   **Torvar**: *"Some of 'em, anyway."*

:   **Farkas**: *"Time to train."*
:   **Torvar**: *"Enough with the training, I want to go fight something."*
:   **Farkas**: *"No fighting, not just yet. Not 'till Skjor says so. You train now."*
:   **Torvar**: *"Easy for you to say. You get to fight."*
:   **Farkas**: *"But before I fought, I had to train."*

:   **Kodlak**: *"How are the young ones coming along?"*
:   **Farkas**: *"Some are too happy to fight. Blood runs hot."*
:   **Kodlak**: *"I remember when you were the same way. The more they train, the more they'll cool down."*
:   **Farkas**: *"I hope so."*
:   **Kodlak**: *"Just have them focus on the calm in the battle. Control the rage, don't let it control you."*

:   **Farkas**: *"What weapon do you like, Harbinger?"*
:   **Kodlak**: *"When I was young, I favored huge swords, much like you. Hard to lift these days, but I still enjoy the heft of a good hammer."*
:   **Farkas**: *"Big swords should always beat little swords."*
:   **Kodlak**: *"Brave hearts beat lesser ones. That's the decider."*

## Notes

- "Farkas" is the Hungarian word for wolf, as well as a given name or surname. Similarly, his brother's name "[Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas")" is the Lithuanian word for wolf.
- Farkas is in the faction [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"). This makes him chase you on sight when you have a high bounty in any given [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds").
- Farkas's class is "[TrainerHeavyArmorMaster](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerHeavyArmorMaster "Skyrim:TrainerHeavyArmorMaster")", which results in mismatches between his skills and his default equipment; for example, while his default weapon is a two-handed one, he is more proficient with one-handed weapons.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. The class has had its skills changed to a basic duplicate of the [CombatWarrior2H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H") class, with an additional point in the Heavy Armor skill.
- Farkas is the only male member of the Circle who does *not* wear the [Wolf Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Armor "Skyrim:Wolf Armor") of the Companions. On occasion though, his armor will randomly change either after certain Companions quests or finding him as a random encounter in Skyrim.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. His outfit was changed from Steel Armor to Wolf Armor.
- During the events of [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), a [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") member will refer to Farkas' status as a member of the Circle by stating the following; "He wears that armor, he dies,", despite Farkas not wearing the Wolf Armor associated with the Circle.
- Farkas has unused dialogue, originally allowing for an option to ask him "What's it like being a werewolf?" he would reply with *"I think there are some things that... oh, wait. Are you trying to trick me? You are not a full-blood yet. We can't talk about that."*

## Bugs

- Farkas is initially armed with a Skyforge Steel Greatsword, but will lose it during [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor#Bugs "Skyrim:Proving Honor"). See that quest's page for details and a solution.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes after [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), Farkas will follow you and there is no speech option that lets you part ways with him.
- After finishing the Companions quest line, he and/or Vilkas may not have a dialogue option to get work from them, thus making the [Purity](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity") quest impossible to obtain.
  - This occurs after taking only one or a few [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch")' heads during the [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor") quest (or not keeping the heads). Fix: Acquire at least four heads total (one to give to quest-giver Kodlak Whitemane, and one each for Farkas and [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") later, and one to keep in inventory when talking to them). If Blood's Honor is already complete, you can return to [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven") for more heads. With at least two heads in inventory, save just before speaking again to Farkas or Vilkas; he will take a head, but you need two still in inventory if you need to talk to the other as well to get around the same dialogue problem. This will make the Purity quest available, and the NPC(s) should give you radiant quests normally after it is complete. See [Skyrim:Purity#Bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity#Bugs "Skyrim:Purity") for more technical details.
- Sometimes Farkas follows you and initiates conversation repeatedly. If you are far enough in the Companions quest line, you can ask him to follow you and then tell him to part ways and he stops.
  - This is due to Farkas being in the faction [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"), meaning he will attempt to initiate dialogue with you if you have a sufficiently high [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") like guards do, but unlike actual guards, he will not turn hostile after the conversation and thus will start a conversation again. Clearing your bounty should resolve the issue.
- Farkas is presumably supposed to be made non-essential after the events of [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), like the other members of the circle, however he is left essential afterwards.

# Skyrim:Farm Overseer's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Dwarven Ruin: Farm Overseer's House | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| None | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachZCell08 | |
| Region | |
| [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Southwestern part of Blackreach | |

Farm Overseer's House exterior

The **Farm Overseer's House** is a small [Dwarven building](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). It is in the southwestern part of Blackreach, west of the bridge to the [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"). The building is devoid of any [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") or [automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons").

### Exterior

Fifteen mushroom patches of various types are growing outside the house, as listed below. There is a [geode vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Vein "Skyrim:Geode Vein") just behind the northern corner of the building, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") next to the mushroom patches on the ground.

### Mushrooms

| Mushrooms |
| --- |
| 4 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap")  3 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown")  3 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool")  2 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort")  2 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita")  1 [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") |

### Farm Overseer's House

The house is a typical deserted Dwemer dwelling. It contains a stone double bed against the west wall, a novice-locked wall [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the left of the bed, and an adept-locked chest on the floor, also to the left of the bed. To the right of the bed is a set of shelves holding a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") and some random Dwemer metal items. Against the north wall is a table and chairs, with two [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") sample, and a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow") resting on the table. A quiver of [Falmer arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow") is on the floor in front of the table. There is a wall shelf behind the table on the north wall holding a random healing [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and a random magicka potion. There are a further two glowing mushrooms growing on the north wall, and another on the west wall. The east wall has a fireplace in the center with an unlit fire. A set of shelves to the right of the fireplace holds various Dwemer metal items. Additional metal items are scattered around the room.

# Skyrim:Farmer (NPC)

## Overview

This article is about farmers in the original version of the game. For the werewolf farmer added by the Dawnguard add-on, see [Farmer (Werewolf)](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(Werewolf) "Skyrim:Farmer (Werewolf)").

| Farmer | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000BD759 |

| Voice Type | [MaleDarkElf](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf") | | |

Bodryn

This **Farmer** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") named Bodryn who is looking to [join the Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Looking_to_join_Imperials "Skyrim:World Interactions").

He wields an [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron") war axe and dagger and wears standard farm clothes.

When you meet him, he will inform you:

:   *"I'm on my way to Solitude to join the Legion. A united Empire is better for everyone."*

After that, he will only say:

:   *"I was born and raised in Skyrim, but the Nords treat us like dirt."*
:   *"I want to be on the right side."*

Sylvian

This **Farmer** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") named Sylvian who is looking to [join the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Looking_to_join_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:World Interactions").

He wields an [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron") sword and dagger and wears standard farm clothes.

If you meet him he will say:

:   *"I'm on my way to Windhelm to join up with the Stormcloaks. Ulfric has the right of it."*
:   *"I may have roots in Cyrodiil, but Skyrim's as much my home as any Nord's."*
:   *"The Empire is in shambles. They've banned the worship of Talos."*

A male Nord farmer

This **Farmer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") [seeking refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Farmer_refugees_after_dragon_attack "Skyrim:World Interactions") with his wife after a dragon attack.

He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and wears standard farm clothes. He also carries a raw piece of fruit or vegetable.

### Dialogue

When you get near him, he will immediately warn you:

:   *"There are dragons about, traveler. Be warned."*
:   **I know. I was at Helgen.**
:   *"Then you've seen them, too. We lost our home, our livestock... We barely have enough gold to get by."*

:   :   **Here you go. (Give 5 gold)**
    :   *"Thank you, traveler. Be safe and don't forget to keep an eye on the sky."*

:   :   **Sorry, I can't spare any gold.**
    :   *"That's okay. We'll find a way to get by. Safe travels."*

If you gave him the gold he will now greet you with:

:   *"Thank you for the gold, traveler."*

A female Nord farmer

This **Farmer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") [seeking refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Farmer_refugees_after_dragon_attack "Skyrim:World Interactions") with her husband after a dragon attack. At other times, she may be [killed](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Werewolf_Kills_Loved_One "Skyrim:World Interactions") by her [werewolf husband](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(Werewolf) "Skyrim:Farmer (Werewolf)").[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")

She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and wears standard farm clothes. She also carries a raw piece of fruit or vegetable.

### Dialogue

When you approach her:

:   *"It happened so fast. One minute the dragon was there, the next it was gone. Everything was destroyed."*
:   **Did you see where the dragon went?**
:   *"No. I was too afraid to look. I don't know what we're going to do now. We have nothing left."*

:   :   **Here you go. (Give 5 gold)**
    :   *"You're too kind. Thank you. Be careful and stay safe."*

:   :   **Sorry, I can't spare any gold.**
    :   *"That's okay. We'll find a way to get by. Safe travels."*

If you gave her the gold she will now greet you with:

:   *"Thank you for your kindness."*

A male Nord farmer

This **Farmer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who is leading his painted cow to a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Farmer_leading_Painted_Cow_to_Giant_Camp "Skyrim:World Interactions") to keep the giants away.

He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and wears standard farm clothes. He also carries a raw piece of fruit or vegetable.

### Dialogue

When you approach him and his cow, he will warn you:

:   *"I'd stay away if I were you."*
:   **Why?**
:   *"I'm on my way to a giant camp and I can't guarantee those beasts won't think you're part of the offering. Keep your distance and you shouldn't have anything to worry about."*
:   **What are you offering?**
:   *"The cow, of course. Others do it differently, but I've found that an annual offering usually keeps the giants away from our livestock. Some think it's superstition, but I believe it works. I've yet to have a giant kill any of my livestock."*
:   **And the paint on the cow?**
:   *"It's tradition. We mark the animal as a way to let the giants know we're giving it to them willingly. Sort of a peace offering."*
:   **Need any help?**
:   *"I have everything under control. Thanks for offering."*
:   **Good luck.**
:   *"Thanks. You take care of yourself, now."*

If spoken to again:

:   *"Either way this ends up, I'm headed to the inn."*

Should the cow happen to die, the Farmer will be in despair:

:   *"My wife's going to kill me when I tell her we'll need to bring another cow."*

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WEFarmerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WEFarmerFaction "Skyrim:WEFarmerFaction"); [Crime Faction so crimes against created actors are registered](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime_Faction_so_crimes_against_created_actors_are_registered "Skyrim:Crime Faction so crimes against created actors are registered") | | |

.jpg)

Farmer

This **Farmer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness. He turns into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") when approached and will proceed to attack. He carries three pieces of [raw meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Raw_Meat "Skyrim:Food").

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Farmer_(Werewolf)&action=edit).*

Farmhand

**Farmhands** are generic workers that you can ask your [Personal Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") to hire for [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation"). Once hired, two of them will work the farm and dwell in the [Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Farm_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse"). If the bunkhouse hasn't been [constructed](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") yet, they will instead set up bedrolls and camp outside.

You can also personally hire [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored"), [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin"), [Embry](/wiki/Skyrim:Embry "Skyrim:Embry"), or [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") instead of the two generic farmhands.

# Skyrim:Faryl Atheron

## Overview

| Faryl Atheron (RefID: 0001B125) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | | |
| House | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") | | |
| Race | [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001B125 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00014131 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 75 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 60 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleDarkElf](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleDarkElf") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Brandy Mug Farm Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy_Mug_Farm_Faction "Skyrim:Brandy Mug Farm Faction"); [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [WindhelmAtheronFamilyFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmAtheronFamilyFaction "Skyrim:WindhelmAtheronFamilyFaction"); [WindhelmCornerclubPatrons](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmCornerclubPatrons "Skyrim:WindhelmCornerclubPatrons") | | |

Faryl Atheron working at the [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm")

Faryl talking with Bolfrida

**Faryl Atheron** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who lives with his brother [Aval](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron") and his sister [Suvaris](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron") at the [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") in the Gray Quarter of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He is employed as a farmhand by [Bolfrida Brandy-Mug](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolfrida_Brandy-Mug "Skyrim:Bolfrida Brandy-Mug") at her [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm") just outside the city gates.

Faryl spends every evening between 8pm and 2am wandering the streets of Windhelm, so he is usually there at the Gray Quarter during the night for [Rolff Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Rolff_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Rolff Stone-Fist")'s loud insults. From 2am till 8am he sleeps at his house. During the day, Morndas through Fredas, Faryl can be found at the steps of [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") where his brother Aval joins him with a drink around 7pm. Faryl works at Brandy-Mug Farm on Loredas and Sundas from 8am until 8pm.

He wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothing"), and carries around the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence_Key "Skyrim:Atheron Residence Key") to his family house along with a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

He sometimes talks about his employer.

:   *"Bolfrida is certainly grating, but she pays well. Thankfully nobody from the city can see me out here."*

He does not share the hatred towards the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") as many other Dunmer do and he will tell you that;

:   *"Farm work is hard work. It's good to relax when I can, but I still have to listen to my brothers*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *harping about "injustices.""*

Although he does like some aspects of his job, Faryl will explain to you that it's not the first job he would have wanted to take:

:   *"Of course working for Bolfrida isn't my first choice. But what else can a Dunmer do out here?"*

He will also tell you about his brother's dislike of how he and his sister work for Nords:

:   *"My sister and I both work for the Nords. Our brother is ashamed of us, but at least we can affort*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *to eat."*

### Conversations

When working at the farm, he can be seen having the following conversations with his employer:

:   **Faryl:** *"I don't think we're going to get those potatoes to come in."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Well of course, not with an attitude like that!"*
:   **Faryl:** *"The ground is practically frozen. We can't dig down far enough."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Come on, we just need a little elbow grease."*

They'll talk about what it would be like to try growing crops in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").

:   **Bolfrida:** *"I'll bet this is better than trying to grow something in Morrowind, though, isn't it?"*
:   **Faryl:** *"Firstly, I've never even seen Morrowind. Secondly, in volcanic soil the plants practically grow themselves."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Oh, my, I hadn't thought of that."*
:   **Faryl:** *"There are places in the world that aren't wrapped in ice, you know."*

They'll also talk about growing crops in permafrost.

:   **Bolfrida:** *"Now, I've been reading about the best ways to grow corn in permafrost..."*
:   **Faryl:** *"I keep telling you, without a warming enchantment, it will never grow past your ankles."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Right, but if you plow the soil with [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts")..."*
:   **Faryl:** *"Then you've salted it and nothing will grow at all. Genius."*
:   **Bolfrida:** *"Oh dear, I hadn't thought of that."*

## Notes

- In one of his greetings, Faryl mentions having to listen to his "brothers", despite only having a singular brother, Aval.
- Version 1.2.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") alters Faryl's schedule so that he works on weekdays and relaxes in the weekend, as opposed to the other way around, based on his dialogue implying he's working most of the time.

# Skyrim:Fastred

## Overview

| Fastred (RefID: 00019E06) | | | |

Fastred

Fastred getting berated by her father

Fastred being told to work a little harder

**Fastred** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") and a resident of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). She lives with her parents, [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti") and [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor"), at [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm"). She harbors dreams of becoming an adventurer, and will pester you for tales of your adventures. However, her dreams seem to be interfering with her work on the farm, as her parents can be overheard chiding her to "pitch in a little more".

She is infatuated with [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius"). Depending on your actions in [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), Fastred's love life can be considerably altered. After initially approaching her and revealing that you have been sent by [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara"), she asks you to confront her parents regarding her wish to be together with Bassianus. She will elope with him to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") if you mention to Bassianus that her mother is supportive of the relationship. However, if you decide to encourage an old love, [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek"), to be more assertive, she will end up with him instead and opt to stay in Ivarstead.

She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). She is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm_Key "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm Key") to the farmhouse, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

## Dialogue

When she is still living in Ivarstead, Fastred will be quick to ask you about your travels.

:   *"Oh! You're a traveler! You must have so much to tell about the world outside this boring town!"*

No matter where she is, Fastred may also greet you with:

:   *"Have anything interesting to tell me?"*

She will also reveal to you how she wishes she could be a traveler and journey across the world.

:   *"I can't imagine how exciting it must be like to journey from place to place. You're so lucky!"*

You can ask her about [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").

:   **Anything you can tell me about High Hrothgar?**
:   *"The Greybeards are a strange bunch. I heard they live their entire life without uttering a single word; can you even imagine?"*

She will close dialogue with:

:   *"I wish I could go with you..."*

### The Book of Love

Fastred with Bassianus

During [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") enlists you to help Fastred resolve her issues with fickle love. When you talk to Fastred, she will ask:

:   *"Are you the one sent by Mara?"*

You can respond in two ways:

:   **Yes. What's troubling you?**
:   *"My parents are being impossible. Bassianus wants to marry me. And I think I love him. But he wants to move to Riften afterwards, and my father won't allow it. He only cares about this stupid town, but Bassianus makes me happier than anyone ever has. My mother's not any help, either."*

:   **How did you know I was coming?**
:   *"I prayed to Mara and she spoke to me in a dream. She said a stranger would appear to help me. Is that you?"*
:   **Yes. What's troubling you?**
:   (Same response as above)

You again have two options:

:   **You sound a little confused.**
:   *"I don't want to choose! They're both so amazing."*

:   **I'll talk to your parents about it.**
:   *"Oh, thank you so much! It's wonderful to have someone around who understands."*

If you speak with Fastred after this, she will urge you to talk to her parents.

:   *"Have you spoken to my parents yet? Please, my love depends on it!"*

Talking to her parents will reveal that she had previously been in love with Klimmek. You can choose to help either Bassianus or Klimmek in their relationship with Fastred. If you convince Bassianus to elope with Fastred, Bassianus will run to her and they will have the following conversation:

:   **Bassianus:** *"Fastred, we must speak."*
:   **Fastred:** *"Bassianus, sweetie, what is it?"*
:   **Bassianus:** *"We must leave. Your father will never approve of us, and I grow weary of this place."*
:   **Fastred:** *"Where will we go?"*
:   **Bassianus:** *"To Riften, my pet. How you'll adore the city."*
:   **Fastred:** *"Oh, and to be with you!"*
:   **Bassianus:** *"I'll make the preparations immediately!"*

On the other hand, if you encourage Klimmek to be more bold and declare his feelings for Fastred, he will run up to her and the following conversation will play out:

:   **Klimmek:** *"Fastred, I have something to say to you."*
:   **Fastred:** *"Klimmek? What is it?"*
:   **Klimmek:** *"I don't want you to leave Ivarstead."*
:   **Fastred:** *"Why not?"*
:   **Klimmek:** *"Because... I would miss you."*
:   **Fastred:** *"But I thought you only cared about your fishing!"*
:   **Klimmek:** *"What good are fish if you have to eat them alone?"*
:   **Fastred:** *"Oh, Klimmek..."*

# Skyrim:Favors

## Overview

**Favors** are [miscellaneous objectives](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") and [activities](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities "Skyrim:Activities") for citizens of Skyrim that typically involve doing a small errand for the quest giver. Completing these favors can increase their [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you, thereby progressing any objective to [assist the people of a hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People "Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People") as part of the quest to become a [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of that hold (except in the Rift – see [notes](#Notes)).

Increasing your [relationship rank](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") with the quest giver implies:

- You are freely able to take any low-value items in the quest giver's home.
- If the quest giver is a candidate for marriage, they will now like you enough to consider [marrying](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") you.
- If the quest giver is a potential follower, they will now like you enough to [follow](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") you.
- The quest giver may allow you to sleep for free in beds they own.
- You have provided assistance to a citizen of their [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"), which helps you become a [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") in that hold—even if the favor is completed before you start the hold's thane quest.

Note that favor quests for jarls usually lead to the beginning of the hold's thane quest, rather than counting as assistance to citizens, and also that people who live in [Orc strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") or travel with [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") do not count as citizens of holds, and so improving their relationship rank does not help with any thane quests.

## Quests

Several of the quests below are [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quests, and some have multiple quest givers. If you have an active objective from a radiant quest, you must complete that quest before you can receive the same quest from a different quest giver; however, you can receive another quest which has the same name but is a different quest, for example if you are on the Delivery (Hillevi) quest you can begin Delivery (Sorex) without any problems.

Some factions have favor quests that you can do for members of that faction. Those quests are not listed here; see the faction pages for details.

### Activities

These favors display no information in your quest log, and with the exception of brawling per the activity [Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!"), are repeatable and can be easily completed without any skill use.

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Fight! Fight!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fight!_Fight! "Skyrim:Fight! Fight!")**: Prove your strength by wagering on a fist fight with another. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Quest all Drunks Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Drunks_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Drunks Have")**: Make a drunk dance for joy. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Collection

In these quests, you have to collect one or more non-unique items and bring them back to the quest giver.

- **[Coated in Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Coated_in_Blood "Skyrim:Coated in Blood")**: Bring a [Daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") to [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol").
- **[Dravynea's Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea%27s_Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Dravynea's Frost Salts")**: Find some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") for [Dravynea the Stoneweaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravynea_the_Stoneweaver "Skyrim:Dravynea the Stoneweaver").
- **[Elmus Favor Quest (berries)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(berries) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (berries)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Retrieve some [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") for [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus").
- **[Elmus Favor Quest (mead)](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus_Favor_Quest_(mead) "Skyrim:Elmus Favor Quest (mead)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Retrieve one bottle of [Ashfire Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfire_Mead "Skyrim:Ashfire Mead") for [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus").
- **[Few and Far Between](/wiki/Skyrim:Few_and_Far_Between "Skyrim:Few and Far Between")**: Help [Ingun](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") restock [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")'s rare ingredients.
- **[Grin and Bear It](/wiki/Skyrim:Grin_and_Bear_It "Skyrim:Grin and Bear It")**: Give ten [bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt") to [Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm").
- **[Halbarn Favor Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Favor_Quest "Skyrim:Halbarn Favor Quest")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find some crafting materials for [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur").
- **[Hilund Favor Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund_Favor_Quest "Skyrim:Hilund Favor Quest")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find fifty [Riekling spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Spear "Skyrim:Riekling Spear") for [Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund").
- **[Helping Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Helping_Hand "Skyrim:Helping Hand")**: Help [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") cure her [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") addiction.
- **[Ice Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Cold "Skyrim:Ice Cold")**: Find five [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") for [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel").
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Ringmaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Ringmaker "Skyrim:Ringmaker")**: Help [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi") make jewelry.
- **[Sealing the Deal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealing_the_Deal "Skyrim:Sealing the Deal")**: Find three [flawless amethysts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst") for [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei")'s engagement ring.
- **[Smooth Jazbay](/wiki/Skyrim:Smooth_Jazbay "Skyrim:Smooth Jazbay")**: Collect 20 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") for [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi").
- **[Stoking the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames")**: Find 10 [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") to restore [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s forge.

### Delivery

In these quests, you have to deliver an item or message from the quest giver to another NPC (or to a particular location). Usually they cause you to befriend the quest giver, but not the person who wanted the delivery.

- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.
- **[Bothela's Discreet Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela%27s_Discreet_Delivery "Skyrim:Bothela's Discreet Delivery")**: Deliver the [Stallion's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Stallion%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Stallion's Potion") to [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") or [Reburrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius").
- **[Climb the Steps](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps")**: Deliver a load of goods up to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") for [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek").
- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Delivery (Hillevi)](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Hillevi) "Skyrim:Delivery (Hillevi)")**: Deliver a bottle of [Nightshade Extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade_Extact "Skyrim:Nightshade Extact") to [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving").
- **[Delivery (Sorex)](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Sorex) "Skyrim:Delivery (Sorex)")**: Deliver a bottle of Rum to [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard").
- **[Delivery to Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Delivery to Calcelmo")**: Deliver a ring to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").
- **[Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute")**: Take Torygg's war horn to the Shrine of Talos.
- **[For the Good of Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:For_the_Good_of_Morthal "Skyrim:For the Good of Morthal")**: Deliver a letter to [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
- **[Gharol's Message](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol%27s_Message "Skyrim:Gharol's Message")**: Deliver [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol")'s sword to [Lash](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh").
- **[Greatsword for a Great Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword_for_a_Great_Man "Skyrim:Greatsword for a Great Man")**: Adrianne asks you to deliver a sword to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), her father.
- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") make peace with her dead father.
- **[Rogatus's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter")**: Deliver a letter to a [farmer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius").
- **[Salt for Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia")**: [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") asks you to deliver some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia").
- **[Skaal Village Dialogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village_Dialogue "Skyrim:Skaal Village Dialogue")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Take [Bera's necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Bera%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Bera's Necklace") to [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
- **[Special Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Delivery_(Bolli) "Skyrim:Special Delivery (Bolli)")**: Deliver a purchase agreement to [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
- **[Special Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Delivery_(Sylgja) "Skyrim:Special Delivery (Sylgja)")**: Make a delivery for [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") to [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing").
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
- **[That Was Always There](/wiki/Skyrim:That_Was_Always_There "Skyrim:That Was Always There")**: Return a [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola%27s_Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Viola's Gold Ring") to its rightful [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano").
- **[Under the Table](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_the_Table "Skyrim:Under the Table")**: Deliver a smuggled Black-Briar Mead keg to the inn at [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").

### Kill

In these quests, you have to kill a person or creature on behalf of the quest giver. Often you will find yourself fighting others as well on the way to the target, who is usually the boss of a dungeon.

- **[Dark Ancestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Ancestor "Skyrim:Dark Ancestor")**: Destroy [Dengeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn")'s risen ancestor, the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") [Vighar](/wiki/Skyrim:Vighar "Skyrim:Vighar").
- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader (Jarl)")**: Slay a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader for [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Giant (Jarl)](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Kill the Vampire")**: Do menial work for [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") by assaulting [a vampire lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave").
- **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)")**: Clear the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") from [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine").[†](#intnote_Clearing)
- **[Mine or Yours](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_or_Yours "Skyrim:Mine or Yours")**: Help [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") by ridding the [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
- **[Nimhe, the Poisoned One](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe,_the_Poisoned_One "Skyrim:Nimhe, the Poisoned One")**: Kill the giant frostbite spider blocking access to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
- **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole_(quest) "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole (quest)")**: Defeat the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole").[†](#intnote_Clearing)

[†](#note_Clearing)While the quest appears to tell you to kill all the enemies in the mine, you only have to kill the boss of the mine to complete the quest.

### Persuasion

In these quests, you have to persuade another NPC of something on behalf of the quest giver.

- **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bullying Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Bullying_Braith "Skyrim:Bullying Braith")**: Convince Braith to stop bullying Lars.
- **[No News is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News")**: Find out about the fate of [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard")'s daughter from [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis").
- **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)")**: End the dispute over [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine").
- **[The Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:The Spiced Wine")**: Convince [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") to hand over some spices.
- **[Stabilized](/wiki/Skyrim:Stabilized "Skyrim:Stabilized")**: Help [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr") clear his debt with [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)").

### Retrieval

In these quests, you have to find something unique (usually just one item) and return it to someone, usually the quest giver. The difference between Collection and Retrieval quests is that in collection quests, you can find the thing you need in several different locations, whereas in these quests you have to go to a particular spot.

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet")**: Retrieve [Andurs'](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") from the [catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)").
- **[Argonian Ale Extraction](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale_Extraction "Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction")**: [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") longs for the taste of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). Can you steal some for him?
- **[Bow to the Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_to_the_Master "Skyrim:Bow to the Master")**: Retrieve a [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dravin_Llanith "Skyrim:Dravin Llanith")'s stolen bow.
- **[Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed")**: Gather three marks of Dibella to help [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") against [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").
- **[Distant Memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Distant_Memories "Skyrim:Distant Memories")**: Help [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") uncover his past.
- **[Dragon's Breath Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Breath_Mead_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragon's Breath Mead (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragon's Breath Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Breath_Mead_(item) "Skyrim:Dragon's Breath Mead (item)") and give it to either [Olda](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda") or [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir").
- **[Dungeon Delving (Bandits)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving (Caves)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Hagravens) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)")**: Do a favor for [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the Jarl of Markarth, by retrieving a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
- **[The Forgemaster's Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forgemaster%27s_Fingers "Skyrim:The Forgemaster's Fingers")**: Find [the Forgemaster's Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forgemaster%27s_Fingers_(item) "Skyrim:The Forgemaster's Fingers (item)") to gain favor with the Orcs. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Grimsever's Return](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever%27s_Return "Skyrim:Grimsever's Return")**: Recover [Mjoll](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")'s beloved sword, [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever"), from [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").
- **[Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather")**: Retrieve [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon"), [ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items"), and [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").
- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").
- **[Search and Seizure](/wiki/Skyrim:Search_and_Seizure "Skyrim:Search and Seizure")**: Find evidence of a [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund") for the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Skilled Apprenticeship](/wiki/Skyrim:Skilled_Apprenticeship "Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship")**: Retrieve a [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash") for [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol").
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Straw that Broke](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Straw_that_Broke "Skyrim:The Straw that Broke")**: Discover what is plaguing [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s mind.
- **[Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences")**: Retrieve an [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") sample from [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar").

### Other

- **[Bloody Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Nose "Skyrim:Bloody Nose")**: Defeat [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") in a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl").
- **[Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian")**: Rescue [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") from his [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") captors.
- **[Flight or Fight](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_or_Fight "Skyrim:Flight or Fight")**: Help [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta") at [Heartwood Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Heartwood_Mill "Skyrim:Heartwood Mill") locate her missing husband.
- **[Lifting the Shroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Lifting_the_Shroud "Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud")**: Investigate the haunted [barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") outside of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
- **[The Lover's Requital](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover%27s_Requital "Skyrim:The Lover's Requital")**: Help [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") locate his former [fiancée](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi"), so he can kill her.

## Notes

- Favor quests in [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") do not provide progress towards becoming [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift"), as that task uses a counter based on completion of [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Riften "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") instead. This includes those that are not Favors, and does not include objectives outside of Riften itself.
- Only one type of these Favor quests can be active at a time:
  - **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving (Bandits)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving (Caves)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
