# Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Convince an [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let a [drunken miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") get back to [the bar](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") |
| Location(s): | [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") |
| Reward: | Enchanted Weapon |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel")) |
| ID: | DLC2RRFavor06 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") | | |

*"What does he care?"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel").
2. Convince [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let Bralsa drink again.
3. Tell Bralsa the good news.

### Bad For Business

Once you have freed the [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") citizens from [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s spell as part of the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") you will be able to talk to a former miner named [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel"). She lives in the [abandoned building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") and can be found browsing the market every day between 8am and 8pm. She has fallen on hard times since [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") closed and has spent all of her fortune made in the mine on drinking [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma") and abusing [Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). When you get near her, she will remark: *"Don't pity me. And don't look at me like that. I know what I am."* You can then ask her why you should pity her and she will explain: *"Doesn't everyone pity the hopeless? Look at me... I'm no better than a beggar."* She then proceeds to explain that she drank her entire fortune away at [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"), or that she used to. When asked what happened she will explain: *"That fetcher Geldis won't even allow me inside. Said I was bad for business. If I want to spend my last bag of coins getting drunk, that's my business. What does he care?"*

### The Concerned Innkeeper

Enter the Retching Netch, locate innkeeper [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") and ask him why Bralsa was banned from drinking at his inn. His explanation will reveal that he did it out of concern: *"Have you seen the poor girl? She's a mess. She used to be richer than Councilor Morvayn and she's spending it all drowning her sorrow. As much as I love making coin, I can't watch her do that anymore. I won't."*

You can then choose between three options. You will need a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill level of at least 50 to persuade him.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| She has a right to do what she pleases. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: I suppose you're right. If she wants to spend her life at the bottom of an ale mug, it's her right. Tell her she'll welcome back anytime. **Failed**: No, sorry. It isn't right. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Bralsa **Failed**: Nothing |
| Let her back in, or you answer to me! **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Okay, okay. There's no need to get violent. If Bralsa wants to come back, she's welcome here... I swear. **Failed**: I'm not afraid of you. She's not coming in here, and that's that. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Bralsa **Failed**: Nothing |
| Maybe this will change your mind. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well, there's morals, and then there's money. In this case, money wins. Tell Bralsa she's welcome here anytime. **Failed**: It's going to take more than that to change my mind. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Bralsa **Failed**: Nothing |

### Back to the Drink

Once you have convinced the concerned innkeeper to let Bralsa drink again, return to her and tell her the great news. She will be quite sarcastic in her response: *"Well then, I suppose I'm off to do what I do best. Here. This was something I carried around in happier times. Maybe you can find a use for it."* She will then hand you an enchanted weapon of the best possible quality as a reward. After that, Bralsa can be found at the Retching Netch every day between 6pm and 10pm, doing what she does best.

## Quest Stages

| Feeding the Addiction (DLC2RRFavor06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Convince Geldis Sadri to admit Bralsa Drel to the inn |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Tell Bralsa Drel she's welcome at the Retching Netch |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor06`.

# Skyrim:Felldir the Old

## Overview

| Felldir the Old (RefID: 0004423B) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Felldir_the_Old "Lore:Felldir the Old")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor"), [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 30 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004423B | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000CDA05 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 388 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 147 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor")**, **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |

| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [Unique](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique "Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [MQAncientHeroFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MQAncientHeroFaction "Skyrim:MQAncientHeroFaction"); [WIAdditem03ExclusionFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WIAdditem03ExclusionFaction "Skyrim:WIAdditem03ExclusionFaction") | | |

Felldir ready to do battle

**Felldir the Old**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), is an ancient hero currently residing in the [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor") in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)"). He was one of the warriors, along with [Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt") and [Hakon One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Hakon_One-Eye "Skyrim:Hakon One-Eye"), who fought against [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"), ultimately sending him forward through time using an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scrolls "Lore:Elder Scrolls"). He was also the architect of their plan to do so.

He and his compatriots later assist you in the final battle against Alduin in Sovngarde. Upon returning to Tamriel, you can summon his spirit using the first two words of the [Call of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_of_Valor "Skyrim:Call of Valor") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

He wears [Greybeard's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Greybeard's Robes") with a pair of [Greybeard's boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Boots "Skyrim:Greybeard's Boots") and is armed with an [ancient Nord greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Greatsword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Greatsword"). He knows the following shouts: [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"), [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form"), [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal"), [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay"), [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm"),
[Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force"), though when summoned with Call of Valor, he will only use Unrelenting Force and Frost Breath in combat.

## Related Quests

- **[Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")**: Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") at the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").
- **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") within [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
- **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the [World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### Alduin's Bane

At a certain point, Felldir the Old will emerge from behind you and join the conversation:

**Hakon**: (To Felldir) *"Why does Alduin hang back? We've staked everything on this plan of yours, old man."*
**Felldir**: *"He will come. He cannot ignore our defiance. And why should he fear us, even now?"*
**Gormlaith**: *"We've bloodied him well. Four of his kin have fallen to my blade alone this day."*
**Felldir**: *"But none have yet stood against Alduin himself. Galthor, Sorri, Birkir..."*
**Gormlaith**: *"They did not have Dragonrend. Once we bring him down, I promise I will have his head."*
**Felldir**: *"You do not understand. Alduin cannot be slain like a lesser dragon. He is beyond our strength. Which is why I brought the Elder Scroll."*

Felldir will then pull out the ancient [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scroll "Lore:Elder Scroll"), much to the surprise of Hakon:

**Hakon**: *"Felldir! We agreed not to use it!"*
**Felldir**: *"I never agreed. And if you are right, I will not need it."*
**Hakon**: *"No. We will deal with Alduin ourselves, here and now."*
**Gormlaith**: *"We shall see soon enough. Alduin approaches!"*
**Hakon**: *"So be it."*

When the three Nords proceed to attack the World-Eater, Alduin will pick up Gormlaith between his teeth and fling her to the right, killing her:

**Hakon**: *"No, damn you! It's no use! Use the Scroll, Felldir! Now!"*
**Felldir**: *"Hold, Alduin on the Wing! [Sister Hawk](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"), grant us your sacred breath to make this contract heard! Begone, World-Eater! By words with older bones than your own we break your perch on this age and send you out! You are banished! Alduin, we shout you out from all our endings unto the last!"*
**Alduin**: *"Faal Kel...?! Nikriinne..."*

A surprised Alduin will futilely breathe fire at Felldir before disappearing into the flow of time, to an unknown era. Felldir, however, knows that the defeat was only temporary:

**Felldir**: *"You are banished!"*
**Hakon**: *"It worked... you did it..."*
**Felldir**: *"Yes, the World-Eater is gone... may the spirits have mercy on our souls."*

### Sovngarde

In the Hall of Valor:

:   **I need your help to defeat Alduin.**
:   *"Alduin escaped us long ago. Today we take our well-tempered revenge. For a hundred lifetimes my heart has burned for revenge on Alduin too long delayed."*

After speaking to Ysgramor:

:   **Gormlaith Golden-Hilt:** *"At long last! Alduin's doom is now ours to seal - just speak the word and with high hearths we'll hasten forth to smite the worm wherever he lurks."*
:   **Felldir:** *"Hold, comrades - let us counsel take before battle is blindly joined. Alduin's mist is more than a snare - its shadowy gloom is his shield and cloak. But with four Voices joined, our valor combined, we can blast the mist and bring him to battle."*
:   **Hakon:** *"Felldir speaks wisdom - the World-Eater, coward, fears you, Dragonborn. We must drive away his mist, Shouting together, and then unsheathe our blades in desperate battle with our black-winged foe."*
:   **Gormlaith Golden-Hilt:** *"To battle, my friends! The fields will echo with the clamor of war, our wills undaunted."*

### Dragonslayer

After you cross the whalebone bridge:

:   **Felldir:** *"We cannot fight the foe in this mist!"*
:   **Gormlaith:** *"Clear Skies - combine our Shouts!"*

After shouting:

:   **Alduin:** *"Ven Mul Riik!"*
:   **Gormlaith:** *"Again!"*
:   **Felldir:** *"We can shatter his power if we Shout together!"*

After shouting again:

:   **Alduin:** *"Ven Mul Riik!"*
:   **Hakon:** *"Does his strength have no end? Is our struggle in vain?"*
:   **Gormlaith:** *"Stand fast! His strength is failing! Once more, and his might will be broken!"*
:   **Felldir:** *"His power crumbles - do not pause for breath!"*

While fighting Alduin he can shout:

:   *"Use Dragonrend, to drag him down!"*
:   *"Die, World-Eater, in despair and fear!"*
:   *"Today you die, your doom has come."*
:   *"You may strike me down, but your doom is near."*
:   *"Now ends this tale, my eternity be damned!"*

After Alduin is dead:

:   *"Our ancient debt for Alduin's reprieve is now repaid - the long night is ended!"*

## Summon Dialogue

When he is summoned he can say:

:   *"I answer the call of the Dragonborn."*
:   *"Lead me into battle."*

In battle, he can yell:

:   *"Feel the thunder of my voice!"*
:   *"You will die for the glory of the Dragonborn!"*
:   *"You are not worthy of Sovngarde!"*

## Notes

- For more information, see the [lore](/wiki/Lore:Felldir_the_Old "Lore:Felldir the Old") page.
- He is [voiced](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_Actors "Skyrim:Voice Actors") by [Paul Eiding](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paul_Eiding "wikipedia:Paul Eiding").
- There are actually three different versions of Felldir, which have mostly similar statistics. The summary provides information for the version of Felldir who is first met in Sovngarde. The other two versions are:
  - Felldir that appears during the quest [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane"): BaseID `000CDA00`, RefID `0004423B`.
  - Felldir that you can summon: BaseID `000923F9` (a different RefID is assigned each time he is summoned).

## Bugs

- Gormlaith and Feldir can end up eternally hostile if you are caught trying to pickpocket either of them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, addresses this issue. The ability to pickpocket them has been disabled.

## Overview

Fellglow Keep

**Fellglow Keep** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), and the mages' leader, [the Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller"). It contains three zones: *[Fellglow Keep Dungeons](#Fellglow_Keep_Dungeons)*, *[Fellglow Keep](#Fellglow_Keep)*, and *[Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber](#Fellglow_Keep_Ritual_Chamber)*.

Part of *Fellglow Keep* and all of *Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber* are only accessible during the quest [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books").

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior

The keep can be reached by following a path from the northern [Valtheim Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers"). Two elemental mages and a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") guard the exterior of the keep. One of the mages is standing lookout on a damaged tower, while the other is standing by a campfire near the main entrance to *[Fellglow Keep](#Fellglow_Keep)*. It is initially locked and requires a key to enter. During Hitting the Books, the flame atronach is to the southwest, near an entrance to *[Fellglow Keep Dungeons](#Fellglow_Keep_Dungeons)*, which is the entrance you will have to enter in order to reach the interior of the keep. Otherwise, the flame atronach will be near the main entrance to *Fellglow Keep*, with one of the mages. There is a long wooden table to the right of the main entrance with a haunch of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a dagger, a quiver of arrows, and a bow on top. There is a small vegetable patch to the east of the campfire. It consists of a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plant, three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and seven [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). There is a [chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") wandering the area, and to the southeast a shallow pool that contains a [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"), or three [goldfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldfish "Skyrim:Goldfish") with the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity) "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). A novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is on the far right side of the first ledge on the main keep tower.

### Fellglow Keep Dungeons

The entry leads into a narrow passage that has suffered quite a lot of damage, with fallen stones blocking part of a short flight of stairs leading down to the east. There is a dresser and a barrel on your immediate left with a common [book](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top, while on your right is a bucket containing two samples of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") fungus. There are numerous barrels and sacks containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") throughout the dungeon and keep. At the bottom of the stairs is an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on the ground. The passage enters a small room that is partially flooded, where a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") is growing on some masonry on the ground, while among some rubble on the right is an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). The passage continues to the southwest, through an open door. There is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in front of the door, with a second bear trap a short way along the next passage. Ahead is another partially flooded room. This next room has a balcony to the left, where an [ice mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") is standing guard with two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") or [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). There are two more Nordic barnacles, three loose [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), and at least four salmon swimming in the flood water. There are many crates and unusable barrels around the room, on the balcony, and throughout the dungeon and keep, with many items of clutter among them. There are stairs along the rear wall leading up to the balcony. In the southern corner is a long wooden table with a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a bottle of ale, a portion of grilled leeks, and an iron dagger on top. Behind the table, among thick cobwebs is a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), while beside it is a counter with two [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a common book on top. In front of the counter is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") and a basket containing a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"). Against the northeast wall is a set of shelves holding a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), five common books, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). To the left is a small square table with two more common books and a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top, while to the right of the shelves are two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood").

To the southeast is a passage leading down a few steps to a T-junction with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") on the ground. This triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from the right. Passageways lead to the left and straight on. The latter ascends a few steps before turning to the right. There is an end table by the turn with a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on top. Around the corner is a closed wooden door into a small room containing an apprentice-locked chest, and a set of shelves holding an [iron cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), a random cuirass, and an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), with a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") in front. Beside the shelves is another small end table with a leather strip on top.

Back at the junction, take care as a few paces along the passage to the left is a [shock rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Elemental Rune") trap on the ground (*Note*: this rune has been reported to be invisible at times, so tread carefully; additionally, if you trigger it from a distance, it may alert the mage in the next room). Beyond this is a food barrel with a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") on top by an open door that leads into a larger room with four cells along the far wall. To the right of the door is a torture rack, and hanging from the ceiling is a small cage. There is a mage around the corner to the right. During Hitting the Books, three of the cells have live captive leveled vampires locked in them; otherwise, the cells contain dead vampires. You can either kill each of the vampires with ranged magic or a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), or if you unlock the cells, they will rush through the door to the southeast and attack a group of mages that have been performing dissections on a pair of [master vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Vampire "Skyrim:Master Vampire"), a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_(dead) "Skyrim:Khajiit (dead)"), and a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"). The vampires will then leave the dungeon without attacking you (unless you attack them first). The cells are all apprentice-locked, and can either be [lockpicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") or opened using the four levers on the southeast wall to the right of a wooden door, each opening one of the cells. The vampires may be carrying useful items, including [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). There is a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer") leaning against the wall by the rack. Under the levers is a dresser with a dagger, a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") on top. To the right of the dresser is a long wooden table holding an iron dagger, a common book, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"); some of these are in a wooden bowl. Beside the table is a set of shelves holding a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a medium coin purse, two common books, a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, and two bottles of ale. Against the northwest wall, beside some rubble from a cave-in is a stack of crates with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") on top.

The next room contains three mages, who will be dealt with by the vampires if you released them; otherwise, you may be in for a difficult fight. There are four wooden tables in the room with experiments on top: two with dead master vampires on top against the northwest wall and in the middle of the room between two pillars, a third with a dead Khajiit on top against the southeast wall, and the final table with a dead Nord on top against the northeast wall. The first three have leveled mages standing beside them. On your right as you enter is a table with a set of working shackles on top, and beside the table against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding four books and a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"). To the left is a passage that has caved in, with a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus growing among the rubble, and to the left of the passage is a crate with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") on top. In the northern corner is a cupboard with two common books and a salt pile on the shelves. There are three small cages hanging from the ceiling; the one in the southern corner has a dead Khajiit inside, while the others contain only bones. Along the northeast wall is a wooden block with an iron dagger and a salt pile on it, another set of shelves holding six more books and a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a dresser containing clothes with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top. In the eastern corner is a wooden door. To the left of the Khajiit against the southeast wall are two more sets of shelves holding four more books, a filled [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus.

Through the door is another caved-in passage, with a flight of stairs descending on your right. At the bottom is a round table holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with the passage opening up to the northeast into another room with cells against the walls. This next room is circular, with one mage on guard opposite by a large fireplace. There is a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on the hearth, and a long wooden table to the right. On the table is an iron dagger, a leather strip, and some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. Opposite the fireplace, against the wall is a set of shelves holding clutter and a random empty soul gem. Beside this is another woodcutter's axe. There are two barrels to the left of the fire, with a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on top. There are three levers in the middle of the room that open the three cells to the east, southeast, and south. [Orthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthorn "Skyrim:Orthorn") is in the southeast cell, and two [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") are in the east cell unless the mage is able to release them to aid him in fighting you. You can choose whether or not to release Orthorn, and even if you take pity on him, you are not required to allow him to accompany you. In the northern corner of the cell containing the wolves is a medium coin purse that is difficult to see due to cobwebs.

There are three doors from this room, not including the entrance you used. The locked door to the west opens into a small storeroom containing an apprentice-locked chest, a sideboard with an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), and a pair of iron gauntlets on top, and a set of shelves holding a common book, a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a salt pile, a medium coin purse, a bottle of wine, and a random potion. At the top of the stairs to the northwest is another dresser containing clothes and a wooden door that leads to *Fellglow Keep* that requires a key to open. The third door to the northeast isn't locked. Behind it is a passage with a bucket on the floor on your left containing a [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster") and a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). After a few paces the passage staggers to the right, by a table with an iron dagger on top. The next section is brightly lit, with a small shelving unit holding a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") and a leather strip. The passage descends a flight of stairs to the northwest. You can hear someone receiving instruction ahead.

The passage turns to the northeast at the bottom, where you will see two mages ahead practicing fire spells while a third mage looks on. There are three target lanes opposite: the one on the right contains a dead vampire in a small hanging cage, the middle one has a practice dummy at the end, and the one on the left has a captive vampire in a small hanging cage. There is long wooden table in the middle of the room with a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* on top. In the southern corner is a cupboard, with seven common books and three food sacks on the shelves. To the left is a dresser containing clothes, with an iron dagger on top. The northwestern side of the room has a slightly raised area, with a cupboard on the left holding five more common books, a sprig of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") in a basket. To the right is a small shelving unit partially buried in rubble, with an iron mace on a shelf. Between these is a flight of stairs; at the top of the stairs is another cupboard, with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on the shelves. The passage turns to the northeast, with a basket on the right holding a leg of goat and two potatoes. The passage continues to climb two more small flights of stairs, opening into a lit room containing two leveled [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and a total of eleven sarcophagi along the side walls. The sarcophagi burst open and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") emerge; some rise, while others are already dead and can be looted. The last sarcophagus on the right also contains a random filled soul gem and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). At the far end is a plinth with a *[Spell Tome: Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Raise Zombie")* on top. Behind this is a twelfth sarcophagus. To the right is a small room where the ceiling has caved in, containing a cupboard with a creep cluster on a shelf, two barrels of ingredients, and a set of shelves holding a random filled soul gem, a leather strip, and two common books. To the right of the shelves is an unlocked chest. To the left of the last sarcophagus is a passage leading up to a door to *Fellglow Keep*.

### Fellglow Keep

Unusual gem

Through the door is a passage, with a dresser ahead with a medium coin purse, a random empty soul gem, and a common book on top. To the right is a flight of stairs leading up to another door. This door opens into another room containing two mages and a [familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Familiar "Skyrim:Familiar") or atronach. There is a damaged altar with a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") that can still be used. Behind the damaged statue is a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") stuck into the rubble. Next to the altar is a plinth with a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")* on top. There are four filled petty soul gems in holders on the floor in a square overlaid with four lit candles, presumably for some form of ritual, while to the right of the square are several wooden benches facing east toward another door.

The door opens into a small room containing a necromancer seated at a table. There is a large fireplace on the right, beside a counter with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a [grass pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), two food sacks, and a cabbage on top. By the fireplace is a flower basket containing a sample of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and a sample of scaly pholiota. There are three small tables with chairs and one long table with a bench in the room; one table has a bottle of alto wine on top. To the north is a wide doorway into a passage. In the northwest corner is a cupboard holding a basket containing three sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). To the right is a dresser. Against the south wall is a crate with a woodcutter's axe on top. The passage heads east, passing a small shelving unit holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a food sack, and a long wooden table with a random potion of healing, a bottle of wine, a portion of grilled leeks, and a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") on top. To the north is an alcove with a locked door to *Fellglow Keep Dungeons*. The door, which cannot be picked and requires a key to open, opens at the top of the stairs in the dungeon where Orthorn was held. On the left on top of some unusable barrels is a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe").

Ahead the passage passes through a door into a room on two levels. You enter into the lower level; to the right is a flight of stairs up to the upper level where you will find a mage and a familiar or atronach. On the lower level are two doors: one to the north and another to the east. The door to the north is the keep's main entrance, but is locked and requires a key. There are two long wooden tables and benches in the middle of the room, and several sets of shelves, cupboards, and a dresser around the room which hold a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of wine, a salt pile, a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower hidden in a cast iron pot, a bowl of bone meal, eleven common books, and a sack of food. There is also a small counter with a cabbage, a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and a sack of food on top. The upper level has a cupboard holding two potatoes, a bottle of ale, and three sacks of food, and a set of shelves holding two bottles of alto wine, two bottles of wine, and two pieces of cheese. If you are on the [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") quest, there will be three doors leading off this level to the east, south, and west. If you are not on this quest or hadn't solved it previously, you will only see the door to the west.

The door to the east from the lower level leads into a dormitory containing two necromancers, six single unowned beds, a dresser, an end table, a tall wardrobe, and a set of shelves. On the shelves are two bottles of alto wine, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a medium coin purse, and three common books. Beside the wardrobe is a bucket containing a gourd. To the south is a passage with two barrels on the right, with a bunch of jazbay grapes in a wooden bowl on top. A dresser on the left has a [briar heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart") on top; around to the left is a common book on a barrel.

To the west from the upper level is a room containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a fireplace. There is a small counter with an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") (related to the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")), an apothecary's satchel, a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, a random potion of magicka, and three pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") on top. There is also a cupboard with a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron"), a hammer and tongs, three [quicksilver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ingot "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ingot"), three common books (including a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, which starts the quest [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")), and two soul gems, one filled and one empty, on the shelves. The door south is barred from the other side. The door to the east opens to a short passage leading to stairs up into a larger room above. There is a wardrobe and a table with a bowl of bone meal on top at the bottom of the stairs. The room at the top has two leveled mages, who may be alerted during previous fights.

The room at the top of the stairs is circular, with passages to the north and south, sets of shelves along the walls around the entire room, and a circle of shelves forming a small area in the middle facing outwards. In the middle of these central shelves are three small tables and chairs, with a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")*, a bottle of alto wine, a piece of bread, a portion of grilled leeks, a bottle of wine, a common book, a small coin purse, and a random potion on top of the tables. The shelves around the room hold many [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a sample of scaly pholiota fungus, a salt pile, two bunches of lavender, several food sacks, a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a sample of creep cluster, a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), two leather strips, a sample of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus, an iron mace, three bottles of alto wine, four bottles of wine, a copy of *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* (which starts the quest [Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") as long as you are level 30), a [hooded black robe](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Robes"), a *[Spell Tome: Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Sparks "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Sparks")*, a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") hidden in a flower basket, and two iron daggers.

The passage to the south turns after a few paces and heads west up a flight of stairs, then opens into another wider passage. There is a cupboard on the right holding only clutter, and a short distance farther along a door on the left opens into a bedroom containing an unowned double bed, a wardrobe containing clothes, an unlocked chest, and a long wooden table with a gourd and a baked potato on top. Farther along the passage is a door ahead, while the passage turns to the north to another door at the far end. The door ahead opens into another bedroom, this one containing two unowned single beds, one of which has a mage sleeping in it, a wardrobe, an end table, and a cupboard holding a leather strip, a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a [swamp fungal pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a bunch of jazbay grapes hidden in a wooden bowl, and two food sacks. There is a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") on the floor in front of the cupboard. The mage carries a copy of the [Fellglow Keep key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep_Key "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep Key").

At the end of the passage are two doors: one to the north, and an adept-locked one to the east that can be opened with the Fellglow Keep Key carried by the previous mage. The room contains a long wooden table holding a baked potato, a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast"), a portion of grilled leeks, a salt pile, a bottle of alto wine, a piece of bread, a piece of cheese, and an apothecary's satchel. There is a small table and chairs in the middle of the room, with a bottle of wine and some bread and cheese on top. In the southern corner is a [shrine of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrines") on top of a dresser, with two sets of shelves to the left. The shelves hold a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of wine, a bowl of bread, a plate holding a dragon's tongue flower and a bunch of jazbay grapes, two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll").

To the east is a door into another bedroom with an unowned double bed coming out from the south wall, with an end table to the left with a small coin purse and a common book on top, and an adept-locked chest and a pair of random boots at the foot of the bed. There is a wardrobe and a dresser against the north wall, with a bottle of alto wine and a leather strip in a basket on the dresser. In the southwest corner is a set of shelves holding a potion, a basket containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus, and a bowl containing a sprig of frost mirriam and a bulb of garlic. Returning to the passage, through the door to the north is a flame atronach and curved stars leading up. By the bottom of the stairs are two sets of shelves holding a bottle of wine. The stairs curve up and around to a door to the southeast at the top. Opposite the door are more shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, two [scrolls of Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Scroll of Ice Spike"), a random [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), a gourd, and two random potions of healing. The door opens into the *Ritual Chamber*.

### Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber

Upon entering the chamber, you will finally find the Caller. Regardless of whether you are sneaking, you will be instantly spotted, and she will initiate a conversation. She is the leader of the group of renegade mages, and is quite upset over your presence and the destruction you have caused. She also possesses the three books required for the quest Hitting the Books that are found within this room. The books you seek are on three plinths: one is in the center of the room, and two are in the center of alcoves behind.

Your options are essentially:

- Fight the Caller: either through certain dialogue options, by attacking her, or by picking up one of the quest books;
- Trade the books for Orthorn: through some dialogue options, the Caller will offer the books in exchange for your companion; if you accept, Orthorn will walk back to the keep, while you may pick up the books and leave without a fight. If Orthorn is not with you, and you tell her "Maybe we can come to an arrangement," she replies that you have nothing she is interested in;
- [Persuade](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") her to give you the books: she will then let you pick up the books without fighting.
  - If you successfully persuade the Caller, Orthorn will act as if you accepted her trade, saying *"How could you leave me here?"* and walking off into the keep.

She will raise a [Frost Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Thrall_(creature) "Skyrim:Frost Thrall (creature)") to aid in fighting you, and will teleport each time you close with her and deal damage; having a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") or raising your own atronach can greatly help in the battle. Once she is dealt with, collect the books *[Fragment: On Artaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment:_On_Artaeum "Skyrim:Fragment: On Artaeum")*, *[The Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:The Last King of the Ayleids")*, and *[Night of Tears](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_of_Tears "Skyrim:Night of Tears")*. The Caller carries a [Fellglow Ritual Chamber Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Ritual_Chamber_Key "Skyrim:Fellglow Ritual Chamber Key") that opens a door to the northwest, where you will find a boss chest with a random shield leaning against it, and a cupboard to the left holding a random helmet, a bowl hiding a bowl of bone meal, a bulb of garlic, a satchel, five [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), a random filled soul gem, a copy of *[The Wolf Queen, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v8 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v8")*, a random potion of healing, and a random potion. Beside the cupboard is a soul gem stand holding a random empty soul gem. To the right of the chest are two barrels of ingredients, and beside them is a stack of crates with a sheaf of wheat, a medium coin purse, and a gourd on top. There are two food sacks among some rubble on the left, and a trapdoor that opens into a room in *Fellglow Keep*. The room has a door that is barred from this side. Through the door is the two-level room passed previously. The door opposite leads outside via the main door that was previously locked.

If Orthorn helped you, after the fight, he may tell you he will stay away from the College for a while, and leave you.

## Notes

- If you enter the keep before Hitting the Books (or are not affiliated with the College of Winterhold), the doorway leading to the library which leads to the uppermost room is blocked by rocks and rubble. The same happens after the quest, after the interior has respawned. However, enemies still spawn on the other side, even though you can't reach them and they cannot reach you. You also can't open the door which leads to the Caller's chamber, as it is blocked by a bar on the other side.
- You cannot clear this location during Hitting the Books, since the boss is disabled for the duration of the quest. If you have completed Hitting the Books, and if the enemies have respawned, a leveled [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") will spawn in the interior of *Fellglow Keep*. This conjurer has the boss tag, so killing them will allow you to clear the keep. (There are a few conjurers, but only one of them has the boss tag.)
- As soon as you turn in the quest Hitting the Books, the upper part of the castle will be blocked, and more enemies will spawn. If you enter through the main entrance to *Fellglow Keep* (after obtaining the key), you end up directly in the living quarters. Right up the stairs is the room to the right with the smithing equipment and enchanter. The other two passages to the upper part of the castle are blocked by collapsed ceilings.
- The room across from the Caller can't be opened unless you have the Fellglow Ritual Chamber Key. This key can't be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket"), and can only be obtained by killing the Caller or by using the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") perk on the vampires' cells in *Fellglow Keep Dungeons*.
- The insurgent mages do not share factions with the permanent atronachs both inside and outside the keep. It's therefore possible for the mages to detect you without alerting the atronachs, or for the atronachs to attack you on their own.
- There is a chest hidden on the outside of the keep. If you climb the cliff the keep is next to, you can drop down to the second level and reach it from there.

## Bugs

- Once you clear the fort, trying to enter it again will cause a crash. This can happen even during the quest Hitting the Books if you try to backtrack from the Ritual Chamber. If you are on the quest, just leave by the exit to the exterior in the chamber.
  -  To avoid this, enter `coc FellglowKeep03` in the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to move to the Ritual Chamber, complete the quest, then use the console again to arrive at the exit (`coc FellglowKeep01`), turn around, and go out the door.

## Maps

- 

  Fellglow Keep Dungeons
- 

  Fellglow Keep
- 

  Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber

# Skyrim:Fellstar Farm

## Overview

|  |

Fellstar Farm

**Fellstar Farm** is a farm in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), located across the road from the lumber mill and south of the bridge to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").

It is the home of [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor"), [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti"), and their daughter [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred"). It consists of one zone, *[Fellstar Farm](#Fellstar_Farm).*

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti")  [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred")  [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor") |

## Related Quests

- **[Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather")**: Retrieve [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon"), [ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items"), and [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").

### Exterior

| Crops | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 10 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  6 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato")  5 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg")  1 [Grain Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling")  1 [Tanning Rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") |

### Fellstar Farm

Kitchen and dining area

Upon entering, you'll find that this small home is laid out with the bedroom area to the right and the kitchen and dining area to the left. To the left of the door, there are three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, and one portion each of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging along the north wall. A respawning food barrel sits in the northeast corner, next to a non-respawning cupboard holding various dishes on its shelves. Another respawning food barrel is in the southeast corner, next to a dining table on the south wall. The table holds a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), one bottle each of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bucket containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). This table also holds [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s satchel, which contains [Wylandriah's spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon") for the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather"). Beneath the table, a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and another pine thrush egg lie on the floor. Above the table are some more hanging ingredients, including another portion of dried frost mirriam, two portions of dried elves ear, and three garlic braids. Next to these are two hanging racks, one of which holds three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") while the other holds three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). On the right side of the table, a respawning meat barrel sits next to a set of shelves holding books, alcohol, and dishes. This includes four bottles each of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and alto wine, and a copy of the books *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")*, *[A Minor Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Minor_Maze "Skyrim:A Minor Maze")*, *[The Cabin in the Woods](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cabin_in_the_Woods "Skyrim:The Cabin in the Woods")*, and *[Rising Threat, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. IV")*. To the right of these shelves is the fireplace, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") at the center and a kettle holding two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") on the right.

Bedroom area

The west side of the house is where you can find the three beds belonging to the residing family. The southwest corner holds [Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor")'s bed, with a non-respawning chest at the foot of the bed. Next to this bed is a non-respawning end table holding one bottle of Nord mead. Along the north wall, [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti")'s bed is in the corner and [Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred")'s bed is closest to the door. Between these beds and the front door is a small table holding one loaf and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), as well as a bottle of alto wine.

## Notes

- The front door has an apprentice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm_Key "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm Key") to which is carried by Boti, Fastred, and Jofthor.
- The front door is unlocked from about 11:50am to 12:30pm by Fastred and again from about 4:50pm to 11pm by Boti.
- A [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") can be found here, which can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.
- Two respawning food barrels sit outside the house, to the right side of the wood pile.
- A [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") can be found in front of the chickens' nests.

# Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Mine: Fenn's Gulch Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fenn%27s+Gulch+Mine)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KarthwastenFennsGulchMine | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 1 |

Fenn's Gulch Mine

**Fenn's Gulch Mine** is a small [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northwestern [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). It contains only one zone, *[Fenn's Gulch Mine](#Fenn.27s_Gulch_Mine)*.

### Exterior

A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), and a [Juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") tree are found outside the mine entrance.

### Fenn's Gulch Mine

The mine only boasts a single silver ore vein. The rest of the mine contains a variety of typical mine clutter: [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), shovels, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and many barrels containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). When you enter the mine, you have a choice of going left or right. If you go right from the entrance, you will come upon the silver ore vein. If you go right from the entrance then left, you will come across a barred area. If you go left from the entrance, you will ascend a ramp and cross a bridge to a platform. The platform holds a bench, a table with a pickaxe, and another pickaxe at the end next to two barrels.

# Skyrim:Fenrig

## Overview

| Fenrig (RefID: 00038288) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | South of [Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow") ([Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold")) | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleUniqueGhost](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleUniqueGhost "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleUniqueGhost") | | |

Fenrig's spectral presence

*"We're together now. And we will be forever."*

**Fenrig** is the [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who was killed just before the battle at [Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow"), now commemorated by [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument"). He was married to [Ruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruki "Skyrim:Ruki"), who has been searching for him near the monument for an eternity. During the quest [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), they will finally be reunited.

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

### The Book of Love

When you locate Fenrig, and explain that his wife is searching for him:

:   **Your wife is looking for you.**
:   *"Ruki? Where is she?"*
:   **West, in the plains over the mountain.**
:   *"We're expected to fight there tomorrow. Gjukar elected to camp here for the night. I don't like it, though."*
:   **Why don't you like camping here?**
:   *"Our fires are visible for miles. We're in a low valley. Sitting ducks."*
:   **Let me take you to Ruki.**
:   *"If she's come this far from home, it must be important. Lead on. I just need to report back to camp by sunrise."*

When the two dead lovers are finally reunited, a brief conversation will take place:

**Ruki**: *"Fenrig! You're alive!"*
**Fenrig**: *"Of course I am. What brings you here?"*
**Ruki**: *"I had heard that Gjukar's men were wiped out. I came to find you."*
**Fenrig**: *"But that battle isn't expected until tomorrow... Ruki, what's going on?"*
**Ruki**: *"I'm so confused. What's happening?"*
**Fenrig**: *"It doesn't matter. I'm here. We're together now. And we will be forever."*

Together they float up into the sky to spend eternity with one another among the stars.

| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") | | |
| Race Details | [Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleEvenTonedAccented](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenTonedAccented") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WIPlayerEnemyFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WIPlayerEnemyFaction "Skyrim:WIPlayerEnemyFaction") | | |

Fenrik

Fenrik is an ex-[Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigil of Stendarr") who has contracted [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"). He is the leader of a Daedric cult and has made a pact with [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") to sacrifice nine of his fellow Vigilants in return for a vampirism cure. He has constructed an altar to Molag Bal within a hidden chamber inside [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

You will be tasked with killing him and his [thralls](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire Thrall") during the related quest.

He wears a full set of [Vigil Corrupted armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Corrupted_Armor "Skyrim:Vigil Corrupted Armor") and wields a random leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), which can get up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality. He also carries two random leveled [potions of restore health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potions"), a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), and his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrik%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Fenrik's Journal").

He knows three spells: [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), and [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh").

## Related Quests

- **[Unholy Vigil](/wiki/Skyrim:Unholy_Vigil "Skyrim:Unholy Vigil")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_Enforcer_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Vigil Enforcer Armor Set"): Investigate the mysterious disappearances of [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").

Feral Vampire

The **Feral Vampire** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") encountered when exploring [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") during the quest [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes"). After entering the secret entrance to the castle, you'll find her with some [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") before you make it to the courtyard. She is instantly hostile to you whether you have sided with the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") or the vampires. She wears [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps"), and a [Ring of Minor Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Minor_Destruction "Skyrim:Ring of Minor Destruction"), and wields an [Elven Dagger of Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger_of_Fear "Skyrim:Elven Dagger of Fear"). She also carries a [journal fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_Fragment "Skyrim:Journal Fragment") which gives a little insight as to why she's down there.

## Related Quests

- **[Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes")**: Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").

Feran Sadri

**Feran Sadri** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [bandit wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") and [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") in [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"). He wears a set of black [vampire armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Armor "Skyrim:Vampire Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Boots "Skyrim:Vampire Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality. He carries random [leveled bandit loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), as well as a 25% chance of carrying 1-9 gold. He sells potions, poisons, ingredients, and recipes.

## Related Quests

- **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**: Choose your side!

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulets of Night Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulets_of_Night_Power "Skyrim:Amulets of Night Power")**: Retrieve the Amulets of Night Power.
- **[Ancient Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Power "Skyrim:Ancient Power")**: Retrieve [vampire parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Vampire_Arm "Skyrim:Ancient Vampire Arm") from varied locations around Skyrim.
- **[Deceiving the Herd](/wiki/Skyrim:Deceiving_the_Herd "Skyrim:Deceiving the Herd")**: Frame the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") for murder.
- **[Rings of Blood Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Rings_of_Blood_Magic "Skyrim:Rings of Blood Magic")**: Retrieve the [Ring of the Erudite](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Erudite "Skyrim:Ring of the Erudite") and the [Ring of The Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_The_Beast "Skyrim:Ring of The Beast").

### Bloodline

When he sees Serana he will exclaim:

:   *"I can't believe it."*

### Ancient Power

The first time you do this quest:

:   **What can I do to help?**
:   *"I've been performing a little research on the Blood Chalice. I believe we can prolong its salutary effects if we infuse it with potent vampiric blood. I've located the petrified remains of an elder vampire. Bring them to me, and I should be able to extend the effects granted by the Blood Chalice."*

:   **I have returned from <Dungeon> with the <Remains>.**
:   *"Wonderful. I'll make the necessary preparations for infusion into the Chalice presently."*

Subsequent times:

:   **What can I do to help?**
:   *"I've located additional petrified remains of an elder vampire. Bring them to me, and I'll extend the effects granted by the Blood Chalice."*
:   *"The potency of the Blood Chalice is beginning to wane. We must infuse it with more power if we are to keep it's fullest effects."*

### Amulets of Night Power

The first time you do this quest:

:   **Is there anything I can do to help?**
:   *"I've located the last known resting place of a set of ancient Amulets of Night Power. They should be among our kind, not laying about unguarded for mortals to find."*

:   :   **What do these amulets do?**
    :   *"The amulets increase the effectiveness of your vampiric powers."*

:   :   **Where did these amulets come from?**
    :   *"Depends on who you ask. Some say Molag-Bal himself gave these amulets to ancient powerful vampire lords. Some say this is just a myth. Harkon disbelieved in their existence, though perhaps he felt slighted they were not already in his possession and only feigns indifference."*

:   :   **Will I be able to keep these amulets?**
    :   *"Of course. I wouldn't be telling you where to find them if I desired them for myself."*

:   :   **Understood.**
    :   *"Good luck."*

Once you return with the amulet:

:   **I've collected all the Amulets of Night Power.**
:   *"Excellent! I'm sure you'll put those to good use."*

### Deceiving the Herd

:   **I heard you might need help.**
:   *"The Dawnguard have increased their operations and have been aggressively recruiting. We need to put a damper on their efforts and give those trouble makers something to worry about other than harassing our interests. You are to make a public show of murdering someone. Do it in the streets for all to see. The higher the profile the better. Make it seem you are a member of the Dawnguard, thus sowing confusion among the herd. Wear this armor and plant this note on the victim."*

:   :   **What do you mean by a "high profile" target?**
    :   *"You know, an important member of society. Someone attached to the Jarl's court, a merchant, a bard, a priest, someone with stature. That will make them all more upset to have one of their citizens slain, and under such flimsy pretense."*

:   :   **So we're pinning the murder on the Dawnguard?**
    :   *"Precisely! The people will put pressure on the Dawnguard who are apparently murdering their fellows without provocation. Their focus will be shifted from us, giving us one less nuisance to deal with."*

:   :   **Understood.**
    :   *"Good. I knew I was sending the right man/woman for the job."*

Once you have killed someone:

:   **It is done. I've slain someone on the streets of <City>.**
:   *"Very good. That should, for a time, direct the people's anger towards the Dawnguard and away from us."*

### Rings of Blood Magic

:   **What can I do to help?**
:   *"I've discovered the whereabouts of a set of ancient Rings of Blood Magic. They belong among our kind, not gathering mold in some vagabond's treasure pile."*

:   :   **Where did these rings come from?**
    :   *"Depends on who you ask. Some say Molag-Bal himself gave these rings to ancient powerful vampire lords. Some say that is just a myth. Harkon himself disbelieved in their existence, though perhaps he felt slighted they were not already in his possession and only feigns indifference."*

:   :   **What do these rings do?**
    :   *"They increase the abilities of your vampiric powers."*

:   :   **Understood.**
    :   *"Best of luck to you."*

Once you return with the rings:

:   **I've collected all the Rings of Blood Magic.**
:   *"Well done! I trust you'll put those to good use then."*

## Dialogue

When approached he can say:

:   *"Politics bore me terribly, but they're a fact of life here."*
:   *"Life here has many advantages, don't you agree?"*
:   *"Living here, I have access to magic I couldn't possibly imagine before."*

If you are a mortal:

:   *"Look at you, wandering around causing trouble. Precious."*

If you become mortal again:

:   *"You really ought to become one of us again. Bad for your health, otherwise."*
:   *"Quite bold, to return here as a mortal. Some will take offense."*

During [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)"):

:   *"First Serana, now you find a Moth Priest. I'm sure Lord Harkon is very pleased with you... for now."*

During [Kindred Judgement](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgement "Skyrim:Kindred Judgement"):

:   *"You have the bow..."*
:   *"I'm sure your reward will be great for ensuring our Lord's success."*

If you are in [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") form:

:   *"I find it tiring to converse with someone in that form. Too much effort."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **What have you got for sale?**
:   *"You'd be surprised what people leave behind when you burn their village to the ground."*
:   *"I may not have potions to block the sun, but I do have nearly everything else."*
:   *"Oh, I'm sure I have something you'll find useful."*
:   *"Many in the court don't bother with potions, but I keep things stocked just in case."*
:   *"Always a pleasure to serve a fellow alchemist."*

When you exit conversation with him:

:   *"Follow your instincts."*
:   *"Revel in your power."*

## Conversations

:   **[Ronthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ronthil "Skyrim:Ronthil")**: *"Do you... do you need anything, Feran?"*
:   **Feran**: *"What?"*
:   **Ronthil**: *"Can I assist you? You know I live to serve."*
:   **Feran**: *"No, I don't need anything right now. Please stop asking."*
:   **Ronthil**: *"Yes, of course."*

:   **Feran**: *"Ronthil, where is the last batch of alchemy ingredients I asked you for?"*
:   **Ronthil**: *"Ah, yes. That. There were... well, complications."*
:   **Feran**: *"I don't want to hear about it. I want what I asked for."*
:   **Ronthil**: *"Yes, Feran. Of course. I'll see to it."*

## Notes

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the summary for him reads:

:   *"Feran was a powerful conjurer who was frustrated with the limitations of a normal life span. He saw vampirism as a way to escape the confines of that and allowed himself to be turned. He uses his immortality to learn as much as he can. As such, he's not terribly interested in the politics of the court; he provides services so he's seen as useful and can retain access to all of the resources at Harkon's disposal, but he keeps himself removed from the group at large. He's taken on Ronthil as an apprentice of sorts, largely because he knows that no one can stand Ronthil, thus deflecting attention away from himself."*

- Feran shares his surname with [Geldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") and the siblings, [Idesa](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") and [Revyn Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Revyn_Sadri "Skyrim:Revyn Sadri"). How he is related to them is unknown.
