Festus Krex

**Festus Krex** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") found in the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

Festus wears [shrouded robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Robes "Skyrim:Shrouded Robes"), [shrouded hand wraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Hand_Wraps "Skyrim:Shrouded Hand Wraps"), and [shrouded shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Shoes "Skyrim:Shrouded Shoes"), and he carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). He knows a variety of spells, as befitting a mage of his stature. From the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") school he knows [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh"); from the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") school he knows [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), and [Incinerate](/wiki/Skyrim:Incinerate "Skyrim:Incinerate"); from the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") school he knows [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing") and [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward").

He lives a quiet existence in the Sanctuary, getting up at 8am. He'll then spend the rest of the day either sitting around, using the alchemy table or arcane enchanter, or [conversing with his fellow assassins](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Radiant_Conversations "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). Then, at midnight, he'll head to bed for some sleep.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness")**: Confront the traitor among the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.
- **[Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate")**: Assist [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") members in the fight against the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") assault.
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"There's too much of an obsession these days with knives and arrows. You can kill someone just as easily with a well-placed spell."*
:   *"You like creepin' around in the shadows? Magic'll work just as good there as anywhere else."*
:   *"Nobody ever expects a fireball from the darkened corner."*
:   *"Talk to Babette about potions. She's the creepy little girl - can't miss her."*
:   *"Yes, yes. I'm your brother and I'm supposed to greet you respectfully. So "hello." There, satisfied?"*

If he notices you [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") near him, he'll say:

:   *"This how you get your thrills? Feeling up an old man?"*

Topics:

:   **What can you tell me about yourself?**
:   *"Hmph. I like to say I was born with a wand in my hand. Well, not literally - you can see how painful that would have been for mother. But I was a prodigy! Casting simple spells by one, completing complex incantations by three. Resurrecting corpses by seven! Ha! When I was thirteen I accidentally burned down the family home. A bit of lightning gone awry. Ah, but soon after I mastered my gifts. Completely. I went on to teach at the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") - left after two years. Too simple. Too safe. None of them truly understood the glory of the Destruction school..."*

When exiting conversation:

:   *"Remember, fireballs. You can never go wrong."*
:   *"Go, incinerate some poor bastard for me."*
:   *"Yeah, yeah. Goodbye, kill lots of people, Hail Sithis, and all that."*

### Sanctuary

When you first enter the Sanctuary, Gabriella will be taking part in the following conversation:

Quality "family" time

**[Arnbjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnbjorn "Skyrim:Arnbjorn")**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**[Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara")**: *"Ha ha ha ha! Again! Again! Do the part where he tries to buy you some candy."*
**Babette**: *"Okay, okay. Wait. Here we go. "Ooh, you are such a pretty little girl. Would the sweetie like a sweetie? Oh yes, how about some chocolate?" Oh yes, please, kind sir. My mama and papa left me all alone, and I'm so very hungry. I know a shortcut to the candy shop. Through this alley. Oh ya, very good. Very good. My it is dark down here. Oh, but you are so beautiful. Such a lovely smile. Your teeth... your teeth! No! Aggghh!!"*
**[Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella")**: *"Oh Babette, but you are so wicked."*
**Nazir**: *"What about you, Festus? How did that last contract turn out?"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"Oh, yes, please, old man. Regale us with your tales of wizardry..."*
**Festus Krex**: *"Ah, the young and stupid. Always mocking the experienced and brilliant. My contract went very well, I'll have you know. Tried a new spell. Little something I've been working on in my spare time. Came "this" close to turning that priest inside out. Damned messy."*
**Gabriella**: *"And what of your latest, Arnbjorn. Something about a Khajiit? Merchant was it?"*
**Babette**: *"Oh, a big doggy chasing a little kitty! How adorable!"*
**Nazir**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Festus**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Veezara**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"I am not adorable, it was not funny, and he wasn't a merchant. He was a Khajiit monk, a master of the Whispering Fang style. But now he's dead... and I have a new loincloth."*
**Arnbjorn**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Babette**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Festus**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Nazir**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*

When you first talk to him, he'll appear very uninterested, *"Yes, yes, you're the new Family member. Let's make this easy - consider me the cranky old uncle nobody talks to. You go your way, I'll go mine."* From there on you'll get three responses, regardless of which you pick, Festus will shrug you off with a blunt *"Hmph."*

### Mourning Never Comes

:   **What are your thoughts on Cicero and the Night Mother?**
:   *"Their arrival is the best thing that's happened to this Sanctuary in years. Astrid is an effective leader, but we've been rudderless for too long. Scrounging for contracts, abandoning the Tenets. The Dark Brotherhood has been reduced to a group of common cutthroats. Frankly, it's embarrassing."*

### The Cure for Madness

Once you return to the sanctuary, you'll find Veezara injured on the ground. Babette will be tending to him:

*"Boy, did you miss all the excitement."*

**Babette**: *"Just try to relax, Veezara. Let the elixir do its work. You'll feel better, shortly."*
**Veezara**: *"Achh... Thank you, dear. You are most kind. The jester's cut feels as bad as it looks, I'm afraid."*
**Astrid**: *"Damn it, this never should have happened! We knew better. We knew better, and still we let our guards down. Agh!"*
**Festus Krex**: *"I'll admit, even I'm having a hard time disagreeing with you..."*

Speaking to Festus after this scene will have him say *"Boy, did you miss all the excitement."* Once you find evidence to go and hunt Cicero down, Festus will encourage you by saying *"Burn that little jester alive."*

### Recipe For Disaster

At the end of [The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness") Astrid will refer you to Festus by saying: *"There's just one more target before we strike out at the Emperor. Have you by chance heard of the "Gourmet"? Read his cookbook? It's become quite a phenomenon. The Gourmet is scheduled to cook for the Emperor at a special dinner. You'll kill him, steal his Writ of Passage, and assume the roll*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *of master chef. Festus has been spearheading this part of the assassination plan. He's close to uncovering the identity of the Gourmet. You should report to him."*

When you are ready, speak to Festus, who will inform you about the next contract *"There you are. Took your sweet time dealing with Cicero, hmph? Now let's get down to business. Astrid told you about the Gourmet, I hope?"* Once you confirm this, he'll explain further *"Quite so. But first you'll need to learn who he is. Assuming, of course, that the Gourmet actually is a "he." Could be a woman for all we know."* If you react annoyed about the lack of information on the target, Festus will say *"Don't be so petulant! In my, um, investigations, I came upon this. It's a copy of the Gourmet's cookbook. Ah, but not just any copy. It's signed you see! Seems to be a message from the Gourmet to one [Anton Virane](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane"). I've tracked Virane to the keep in Markarth. It would seem he's the cook."* If you instead ask him if he has any idea to find out the Gourmet's identity, he'll say *"Ah, indeed I do! Indeed I do! In my, um, investigations, I came upon this. It's a copy of the Gourmet's cookbook. Ah, but not just any copy. It's signed you see! Seems to be a message from the Gourmet to one Anton Virane. I've tracked Virane to the keep in Markarth. It would seem he's the cook."* If you didn't react to Festus, and instead stayed quiet, he'll react pleased *"You know, maybe I was wrong about you after all. Anyone who's smart enough to shut up and listen can't be all bad. In my, um, investigations, I came upon this. It's a copy of the Gourmet's cookbook. Ah, but not just any copy. It's signed you see! Seems to be a message from the Gourmet to one Anton Virane. I've tracked Virane to the keep in Markarth. It would seem he's the cook."* From there on you can ask if he's sure Anton Virane knows the Gourmet's identity, to which he'll confirm, saying *"I believe so. Therefore, you are to obtain that information from Virane - who the Gourmet really is, and where he can be found. Oh, and when you're done with Virane, kill him. Loose ends and all that. Next, you'll have to... Are you still paying attention?"* Again you are presented with options, each option results in him continuing *"Hmph. As I was saying... You'll need to kill the Gourmet, of course. But what's more, you'll need to get his Writ of Passage, so you can take his place. Oh, and if you can, hide his body. The longer it takes for anyone else to determine his real identity, the better. Now off with you!"* While you leave, he'll remind you once of your target *"Remember, the Markarth Keep. That's where you'll find Anton Virane. Probably cooking up all of the Gourmet's recipes, passing them off as his own."*

You can also ask for some for info on his book *""Uncommon Taste." It was published a few years ago, and became a sensation throughout the Empire almost overnight. The recipes were hailed as both practical and decadent. I've made a few of the Gourmet's dishes myself, actually. His roast mutton with Redguard berry sauce is to die for. But his chocolate pate gives me the runs."* Asking him if the Gourmet is in Skyrim will have him say *"Yes. [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro"), on orders from [his father](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro"), arranged for the Gourmet to come to Skyrim months ago. To serve as the Emperor's personal chef. But the Emperor canceled his journey at the last minute. Maro was smart, kept the Gourmet around, in case things changed. And so, the Gourmet has remained in seclusion, somewhere in Skyrim... on indefinite hold. Probably feels like a prisoner. But you'll fix that."*

If you speak to him after this, he'll just remind you of your orders: *"Come now, you've got your orders. What else could you possibly need?"*, and *"All you've got to do is find and kill one lousy chef. The clock is ticking..."*

After you've finished off the Gourmet and returned to Festus, he will say *"So, the prodigal murderer returns. And the Gourmet?"* You will then inform him that the Gourmet is dead, but his response will differ based on the optional task you chose to complete or didn't complete. If you did everything perfect, his response will be *"So I gathered. It seems a certain Orc has disappeared. Which means you not only killed the Gourmet, but disposed of the body as well. You've got the Writ of Passage too, I see. Splendid, splendid... Ah, and word has come in from Markarth that the keep's cook has met an untimely demise. You performed your duties to the letter."* You will gain three responses once more, all of them leading to Festus giving you your bonus and same rarely-seen respect *"Hmph. I was wrong about you. I see that now. Maybe we all were. Here's your payment. And... a little something else, as well. From me. Consider it my way of apologizing. For being so damned curmudgeonly! It's called the [Nightweaver's Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightweaver%27s_Band "Skyrim:Nightweaver's Band"). I wore this for years. I want you to have it now. It'll give your magic and sneakiness some much needed "oomph." Now, you'd better get a move on and see Astrid. It's time! Time for the final stage of this grand and glorious operation."*

If you didn't hide the body, Festus will be angry with you, saying *"Good, good. And you've got the Writ of Passage, too, I see. So there's that. I've also received word from Markarth. It would seem Anton Virane has suffered an untimely fate, as well. Good. But unfortunately, that inn is abuzz with the news of somebody killing one of their guests! What, hiding the body was too much for you to handle? Bah! Useless. Here's your gold. Now go see Astrid. The time to move against the Emperor has finally come. Sithis help us all."*

If you tell Festus that the Gourmet is dead but you don't have his [papers](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet%27s_Writ_of_Passage "Skyrim:Gourmet's Writ of Passage") with you, Festus will be upset *"Good. And his Writ of Passage? Oh wait, let me guess - you don't have them. Fool! Amateur! Without those papers you'll never be able to present yourself as the Gourmet! Off with you! Back to the body to retrieve them!"*

If the Gourmet is dead, you have the papers, but you didn't kill Anton Virane, he'll go on a similar rant *"Good, good. And you've got the Writ of Passage too, I see, so that's done. But why? Why, pray tell, have I received word that Anton Virane is still walking around Markarth, hale and healthy as the day he was born? Back to Markarth with you! Virane must be silenced! He's a potential witness, you witless dagger jabber!"*

If Festus sent you back for some reason, speaking to him once you return will have him say *"Ah, you're back. Ready to try again, are we? Let's start from the top. You were sent to kill the Gourmet. And he is..."* Telling he's dead will have Festus relieved, but he'll also feel haste to send you to Astrid *"Right, which we had already established. And you managed to hide the body as well? Good. You've got the Writ of Passage too, I see. So there's that. And Anton Virane has suffered an untimely fate, as well. Good. Well, looks like you completed the contract as directed. Finally. A little sloppy, but, well... done is done. Here's your gold, with a little extra for hiding the body. Now go see Astrid. The final stage of the contract has come. The Emperor must fall."*

If you completed the quest perfectly, Festus will greet you happily afterwards. *"Ah, good to see you, brother/sister. Gearing up to kill the Emperor? Exciting times. Exciting times, indeed."* Otherwise, he'll say *"Look. I gave you a contract, and you completed it. Barely. Now let's go back to you being insufferable, and me being... me."*

### Death Incarnate

When you finish [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"), and return to Sanctuary, you will find Festus' body pinned to a tree by numerous arrows, just outside of the entrance.

A very bad sign

### Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!

During Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!, you will be sent to kill every Dark Brotherhood member in the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), Festus will be one of the required people to kill. During this quest, his normal spells get replaced in favor of [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Flame Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Cloak "Skyrim:Flame Cloak"), [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh"), [Greater Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Ward "Skyrim:Greater Ward"), [Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Grand Healing"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward") and [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"). His iron dagger will get replaced by a steel one and he will also carry leveled gold as well as one leveled restore magicka potion.

## Quest-Related Advice

| [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") | *"Yes. Just because you're now a professional assassin, don't think you have to skulk around in the dark like a skeever and stab people. Do what I do. Walk up to your target, introduce yourself, melt their skin off, and then run like the wind. Works every time."* |
| [Whispers in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispers_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:Whispers in the Dark") | *"Ha! And would that surprise anyone? This Sanctuary's a mess. Wouldn't surprise me if somebody's talking to the fool on the sly. Making deals. And no, before you ask, it's not me. I know which side my bread is buttered on."* |
| [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") | *"So you're the Listener, hmm? Well that hardly seems fair. You just got here. The Night Mother should have spoken to me. Any idiot could see that. But, I will serve gladly, as that's my lot in life. Now let's see. Ah yes, Volunruud. It's an old crypt, infested with Draugr. So plan accordingly. "* |

I should know, I killed a bride once. It was our honeymoon. Tepid, I said! The bathwater should be tepid! Lukewarm is not tepid! Close, maybe, but there's is a difference! Stupid cow."* |

While it's true I prefer sorcery's more destructive nuances, we mustn't forget the many spells with simpler, more practical applications. Sure, you poison the Emperor, but what then? Why not summon an Atronach to cause some chaos? Or turn invisible and slip away. Use your imagination!"* |

## Notes

- Festus is an essential NPC until he suffers a scripted death. His corpse is actually considered a container in game data (Form ID: `00075CE6`). There is also game data for another dead version of Festus Krex (Base ID: `000E0D6F`), though this version is not used at all in the game.
- Festus' corpse will remain pinned to a tree just outside the door of the sanctuary for the remainder of the game after [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate").

# Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Fetch a book for [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |
| Location(s): | [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") |
| Reward: | Small amount of leveled gold [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") (if not already) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Urag) (MGR20B only) |
| ID: | MGR20, MGR20B |

Urag gro-Shub wants you to find books for the Arcanaeum.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
2. Retrieve the requested book.
3. Return to Urag gro-Shub.

### The Arcanaeum

After joining the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), you will find an opportunity to visit [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). Here you will meet the master archivist, [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). He is very solicitous of his books, threatening bodily harm should any problems arise under his watch. After his blustering, ask Urag if there is any College business you can help with. If you assure him you are feeling adventurous, he will name a book title he would like to procure from a more "dangerous" location.

### Reading List

The book that you are asked to find is randomly selected from the following list:

- *[Arcana Restored](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcana_Restored "Skyrim:Arcana Restored")*
- *[Brothers of Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Brothers_of_Darkness "Skyrim:Brothers of Darkness")*
- *[Children of the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_Sky "Skyrim:Children of the Sky")*
- *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")*
- *[Chronicles of Nchuleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Chronicles_of_Nchuleft "Skyrim:Chronicles of Nchuleft")*
- *[Cleansing of the Fane](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_of_the_Fane "Skyrim:Cleansing of the Fane")*
- *[Fragment: On Artaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment:_On_Artaeum "Skyrim:Fragment: On Artaeum")*
- *[Glories and Laments](/wiki/Skyrim:Glories_and_Laments "Skyrim:Glories and Laments")*
- *[Hanging Gardens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Gardens "Skyrim:Hanging Gardens")*
- *[Invocation of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Invocation_of_Azura "Skyrim:Invocation of Azura")*
- *[Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:Last King of the Ayleids")* — (**NOT** the similarly named *[**The** Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:The Last King of the Ayleids")*, even though the text is identical.)
- *[The Legendary Scourge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legendary_Scourge "Skyrim:The Legendary Scourge")*
- *[Souls, Black and White](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls,_Black_and_White "Skyrim:Souls, Black and White")*
- *[N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!](/wiki/Skyrim:N%27Gasta!_Kvata!_Kvakis! "Skyrim:N'Gasta! Kvata! Kvakis!")*
- *[The Old Ways](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Old_Ways "Skyrim:The Old Ways")*
- *[Remanada](/wiki/Skyrim:Remanada "Skyrim:Remanada")*
- *[War of the First Council](/wiki/Skyrim:War_of_the_First_Council "Skyrim:War of the First Council")*
- *[The Waters of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Waters_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Waters of Oblivion")*
- *[The Wild Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wild_Elves "Skyrim:The Wild Elves")*
- *[The Wolf Queen, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v6 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v6")*

The book will be located in the boss-level chest of any [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") in the game, and as this is a radiant quest, your destination is randomly selected from over one hundred forty possible dungeons.

### A Means to an End

The book you are asked to find is never a skill book, and the monetary reward you get from Urag for returning a book is very small in proportion to the amount of work required to fetch it. However, this quest is a useful means for locating dungeons in Skyrim. The various loot you find in the dungeons will be considerably more valuable than the book.

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- The two different quest IDs correspond to two nearly identical quests. In particular, the lists of possible books and lists of possible dungeons are the same for both quests. The only difference is Urag's dialogue throughout the quest.

## Bugs

- If you find the book before activating the quest, you will be stuck with it. The quest will point to the chest, and the book won't be there, and can't be returned. Once this has happened, you will be stuck with any additional copies you pick up as well, even if you activate the quest before getting a second copy.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  -  Use `player.drop "book ID" "quantity"` to drop and retake the book to complete the quest.
  -  Alternatively use console `player.additem 72841 1` to add quest version of that book to inventory. Then use `setstage MGR20 20` to finish that stage of quest.
- If there is no quest marker pointing you to the book's location, the book may be located in [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"), in which case the book can not be reached until the quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") begins.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The quest marker may point to the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") instead of [Shadowgreen Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowgreen_Cavern "Skyrim:Shadowgreen Cavern"), which is right next door.
- If you find the book before activating the quest, the quest will point you to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") saying "Return the book to Urag gro-Shub" (if you have installed the unofficial patches) but Urag gro-Shub will not provide new dialogue thus making it impossible to complete the quest.
  -  Use `setstage MGR20 200` to finish the quest. (use this if `setstage MGR20 20` doesn't work). Use "MGR20B" if "MGR20" doesn't work.

Complete find book of azura SetObjectiveCompleted MGR20B 10 1

- Urag may not give you a note on the book's title and location, even though he claims you'll get one. Your journal will still be updated, though, and the quest will proceed as normal. **?**

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest quest`.

# Skyrim:Fetch the Netch

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Obtain five samples of [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly") for [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth") |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | Two [Potions of Ultimate Well-being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Well-being") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth")) |
| ID: | DLC2RRFavor02 |

Kill it!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth").
2. Obtain five samples of [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly").
3. Return to Milore Ienth for your reward.

### Hunt for Jelly

The residing apothecary and [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") trainer in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth"), sells a wide variety of exotic ingredients, all of which she grows and harvests herself. However, due to the harsh terrain and the dangers outside the [Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark"), she has problems gathering [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly"). Tell her you are willing to help and she will immediately promise you a reward if you bring back five samples.

The netch jelly samples are dropped by the peaceful, but potentially dangerous, [netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch") that can be found all over [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you have started (or completed) the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") you can gather the only two harvested samples of jelly in Solstheim, specifically deep within [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"), on an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). However, you will either need to visit an apothecary or go netch-hunting for the rest of the samples. The table below shows all fixed locations of the netch, which often reside in familial groups:

The largest netch family

| Location | Bulls | Betties | Calves |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| The river south of the [silt strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Silt_Strider "Skyrim:Silt Strider") | 1 | 1 | 2 |
| The coast near the [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") graveyard | 1 |  | 1 |
| Near [Hrodulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf "Skyrim:Hrodulf")'s corpse | 1 | 1 | 1 |
| North of [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House") | 1 | 1 | 2 |
| The waterfall north of the [Water Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Water_Stone "Skyrim:Water Stone") | 1 | 2 | 3 |
| Off the coast from [Haknir's chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)") | 1 | 1 | 1 |
| Inside [Coldcinder Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Coldcinder_Cave "Skyrim:Coldcinder Cave") |  | 1 | 2 |

Once you have gathered five samples of netch jelly, return to Milore and hand them over. She will be impressed and say, *"Goodness, it must have been quite difficult tracking those creatures down out there. Here, take these. They should help you during your journeys."* She will then hand you two [Potions of Ultimate Well-Being](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Well-being "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Well-being"), ending the quest.

## Notes

- If you already have five samples of netch jelly in your inventory when starting the quest, Milore will say, *"My goodness, you're quite resourceful aren't you? This is all I can offer in return for this. I hope it's enough."* This ends the quest right away.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor02`.

Fethis Alor

**Fethis Alor** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") living in [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") at [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). He is a general goods merchant who will sell various types of items, and requests that you locate [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for him. He has a daughter named [Dreyla](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreyla_Alor "Skyrim:Dreyla Alor"), who helps him run his shop.

Fethis wears a [Dunmer outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") with [Dunmer shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Shoes "Skyrim:Dunmer Shoes"), and he carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House_Key "Skyrim:Alor House Key") to his house, and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

He gets up early at 6am to eat a two-hour breakfast with his daughter in his house. Then at 8am, he heads out to his stall and works for twelve hours. At 8pm, he will close the shop and heads to [the Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") to drink for four hours. At midnight, he either heads to the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone") to work for six hours, or if the stone has been [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), he heads to his house to finally go to sleep.

## Related Quests

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**: Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for Fethis Alor.
- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").

## Dialogue

His greetings are:

:   *"Want to buy anything, or just laugh at our misfortunes?"*
:   *"I'd be on the first ship off of this island if I had the coin. What a waste."*
:   *"If you're looking to buy, then I'm looking to sell."*
:   *"Yeah, so. What can I get you? Got everything from potions to pitchforks."*
:   *"It's busier now that things are starting to look up. I guess I might stay a bit longer after all."* **(If you've helped Raven Rock get [back](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") [on its](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead") [feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold"))**

Once he's free from [Miraak's](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") control, he'll say:

:   *"Being freed from building the shrine... I don't even know how to begin to thank you."*

If he is at the Earth Stone when it is cleansed he will say:

:   *"If I could only get my hands on Miraak. I'd make him pay for playing with my mind."*

When spoken to directly he can be asked questions:

:   **What exactly do you sell here?**
:   *"The question you should be asking is "what don't I sell here" because I have pretty much any supplies you might need. If it's not a weapon, potion or armor, then it's likely that I have it."*

    :   **Where did you get all these items?**
    :   *"[Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjalund_Salt-Sage "Skyrim:Gjalund Salt-Sage") over at the docks brings me most of my supplies, and the rest comes from bartering with the people in town. Oh, [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") gets me a few things once in a while. He usually has the most amazing deals that I can't pass up."*

:   **Are sales that bad out here?**
:   *"Bad? What if I told you that you're the first person that's even considered looking at my wares today. I've half a mind to contact my friends at the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") and see if they need an extra hand in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")."*

    :   **You have friends at the East Empire Company?**
    :   *"Oh, absolutely. In fact, I've corresponded with [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") herself more than once. You know, the lady who runs the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")... the biggest warehouse they have in Skyrim."*

        :   **Okay.**
        :   *"Bah, you're just like the rest of the folks around here. Mark my words... the East Empire Company will return to Raven Rock, and when they do, I'll be at the top of their list."*

Once the mines are [reopened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"):

:   **How are things now that the mines are open again?**
:   *"Things are picking up... for now. All I'm wondering is how long it'll take for House Redoran to begin ignoring us again if the mine runs out of ore for a second time."*

When exiting conversation, he may say:

:   *"If you need any supplies, you know where to find me."*

### Dragonborn

When asked about the shrine outside of town during [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)"):

:   **What's being built outside of town?**
:   *"There's a shrine at the Earth Stone. It's... I'm not really sure what it's for. I thought I knew at one point."*
:   **Why build a shrine outside of town?**
:   *"I don't know... Did we build that?"*

:   **Do you know someone called Miraak?**
:   *"I think maybe I had a dream about someone with that name..."*
:   **Tell me about your dream.**
:   *"It was very strange. Was I... building something? A shrine, down on the beach near the Earth Stone? I'm not sure."*

### It's All In the Taste

When asked if he [wants a drink](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste") from [Geldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), he'll gladly accept:

:   **Geldis Sadri wants you to try his new drink.**
:   *"Geldis needs to bottle this up and send it to the mainland instead of wasting his time out here... his drinks are outstanding. Thanks."*

### Reluctant Steward

If you ask him if he wants to be [Neloth's](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"), he'll immediately decline but point you in the right direction:

:   **Do you want to be the new steward of Tel Mithryn?**
:   *"Don't be ridiculous. Who would run this place? You should ask around at The Retching Netch. Someone there might be crazy enough, or drunk enough, to do it."*

### Pain in the Necklace

:   **Do you sell any special mining gear?**
:   *"Mining gear? No. However, I used to sell [East Empire Pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") until I ran out of them. Popular little item."*
:   **What's an East Empire Pendant?**
:   *"It's an amulet that was made exclusively for the East Empire Company. They gave them to their workers as an incentive at one point... a kind of reward for extra effort. They're no longer being made, so they've become collectible. I'd love to get my hands on a few of them."*
:   **Where can you find them?**
:   *"They could be anywhere on the island. The [mines](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") might be a good place to start. If you find any while you're exploring Solstheim, bring them here and I'll pay you for them."*

When you bring a pendent for the first time, he'll say:

:   *"Well, well. Seems you're proving fairly useful for an outlander. Here's your coin. Keep bringing me more, and I'll keep paying you for them."*

After that, when you turn pendents in he can say:

:   **Still buying East Empire Pendants?**
:   *"I'm beginning to like this partnership. Here you go."*
:   *"As long as you keep bringing them, I'll keep buying them."*
:   *"You're making my buyer happy. Keep them coming."*
:   *"I am. Here you go."*
:   *"Absolutely. Here's your payment."*

During this quest, he may remark when exiting conversation:

:   *"The East Empire Pendants are scattered all over, so leave no stone unturned."*

## Conversations

He can often be seen conversing with other Raven Rock citizens:

:   **Fethis**: *"I never got a chance to thank you for everything you've done. Ever since your mother died..."*
:   **Dreyla**: *"You don't need to say anything, father. I miss her too."*
:   **Fethis**: *"Had we only left a day earlier... she'd still be with us. It's my fault she's dead."*
:   **Dreyla**: *"It was her time, father. None of us have any control over that. You mustn't blame yourself."*

:   **Fethis**: *"Dreyla! I told you I didn't want you seeing [him](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") anymore. Must I lock you into the house at night?"*
:   **Dreyla**: *"Father, Captain Veleth and I are in love. He means everything to me. Am I to simply ignore my own heart?"*
:   **Fethis**: *"He's twice your age and only wants to marry into our family to use my contacts at the East Empire Company. No, I won't allow it."*
:   **Dreyla**: *"Your precious "contacts" have yet to conjure up a scrap of food or work for us, father. Don't make me choose, father... I beg you!"*

:   **Fethis**: *"I want you to stay away from my daughter!"*
:   **Veleth**: *"What Dreyla chooses to do is her concern, not yours."*
:   **Fethis**: *"She has no idea what she's getting herself into. You may not always be there to take care of her."*
:   **Veleth**: *"Fethis, all of us mourn your wife's passing. Just don't let it affect how you treat your daughter."*

:   **Fethis**: *"Geldis, I want you to let me know if you see Dreyla with Captain Veleth. I don't trust him."*
:   **Geldis**: *"She's not a little girl anymore, Fethis. When are you going to let her go?"*
:   **Fethis**: *"He's twice her age and they barely know each other. You expect me to ignore them?"*
:   **Geldis**: *"Raven Rock doesn't offer much in the way of companionship. You should be happy for her."*
:   **Fethis**: *"How about you keep serving the drinks, and I'll decide what's right for her!"*

:   **[Milore](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth")**: *"How's business today, Fethis?"*
:   **Fethis**: *"Haven't sold much. It's going to be a long time before things ever get back to the way they were... if ever."*
:   **Milore**: *"Have faith. Things will change for the better."*
:   **Fethis**: *"Thanks, Milore. I appreciate that."*

:   **Fethis**: *"Milore, I've finally gotten that letter back from the East Empire Company."*
:   **Milore**: *"Gods. Not this again."*
:   **Fethis**: *"What's that supposed to mean?"*
:   **Milore**: *"Fethis, they doesn't*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *care about us. If they did, we wouldn't be standing ankle-deep in ash trying to sell a few meager trinkets to survive. They just send you those promises to keep you off their backs... you must know this."*
:   **Fethis**: *"Sorry, I... Never mind."*

:   **Glover**: *"Fethis! How's that pretty young daughter of yours doing?"*
:   **Fethis**: *"What in the name of the [Black Hands](/wiki/Lore:Mephala "Lore:Mephala") is that supposed to mean?!"*
:   **Glover**: *"Nothing... I... I was just making conversation."*
:   **Fethis**: *"Next time you feel like having a conversation, talk to someone else."*

:   **Fethis**: *"[Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)")... I got those special poisons you asked for."*
:   **Mogrul**: *"Why don't you say that louder so the entire town can hear you, idiot. Just give them to me and put it on my account."*
:   **Fethis**: *"About your account... it's been a few months..."*
:   **Mogrul**: *"I said to put it on my account and that's the end of it. Understand?"*

:   **Fethis**: *"[Adril](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano"), a word please."*
:   **Adril**: *"Fethis, I'm quite busy at the moment..."*
:   **Fethis**: *"Why hasn't a Redoran Guard been posted at my shop like I've requested?"*
:   **Adril**: *"You and I both know we can't spare anyone right now. I don't care if you still have friends at the East Empire Company or not. They abandoned us long ago, so your contacts are meaningless here. That's it."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Fethis' [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") |  |
| ~4 | [Netch Leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather") | Max 5 (5@75) |

The random books he sells are chosen from one of the following lists.

| --- | --- |

| [List 2](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_2 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 2") | 30% |
| [List 3](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_3 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 3") | 20% |
| [List 4](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List_4 "Category:Skyrim-Dragonborn-Books-List 4") | 10% |

## Notes

- In his basement, the [first](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:First Letter from EEC"), [second](/wiki/Skyrim:Second_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:Second Letter from EEC"), and [third letters from the EEC](/wiki/Skyrim:Third_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:Third Letter from EEC") make it clear that this is not quite the friendship he holds it out to be.
- Even if [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") is completed, Fethis' dialogue about [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") doesn't change, and he still refers to her in the present tense. Additionally, there is no dialogue option for you to inform Fethis about Vittoria's fate.
- Between 8pm and midnight (when he can be found at the Retching Netch), he will not buy and sell goods but he will still trade East Empire pendants for gold.

## Bugs

- Fethis' line during Reluctant Steward should say "You should ask around at The Retching Netch." However, the word "should" is not spoken, making it grammatically unsound.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. The line and its matching subtitle have now been altered to say "Ask around at The Retching Netch.".
- Fethis is unaffected by the [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader") perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Despite it being clear in-game that he is the father of Dreyla, the game data incorrectly has them set up as husband and wife.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Few and Far Between

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Ingun](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") restock [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")'s rare ingredients.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") - [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs") |

Ingun practicing

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar").
2. Gather 20 [Deathbells](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 20 [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") and 20 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade").
3. Return them to Ingun.

### The Black Sheep

Ingun Black-Briar has fallen far from the Black-Briar tree. Instead of learning the family business with her brother, [Sibbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar"), she can be found devising alchemical recipes in [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"). The quality of her experiments seem to indicate a dark nature in this well-to-do girl, as she will allude to when speaking to her. Indeed, the ingredients she has depleted from [Elgrim's](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") stores are used to make some very powerful poisons.

### Helping Out

Whether you speak to Ingun in Elgrim's Elixirs or find her walking through Riften, rouse her from her musings and ask her if she is an alchemist.
She will reply: *"I'm aspiring to earn that title, yes. However, the road ahead is paved with loose cobbles and deadly pitfalls. Master Elgrim says I'm a natural; that I have a unique talent. But I fear his approval masks his intolerance for my mistakes. My errant formulas have cost Master Elgrim a fortune in ingredients; some of which are almost irreplaceable."*

You are a helpful sort, so ask: "What sort of ingredients do you need?"
Ingun will tell you: *"To restore Master Elgrim's supply I would need 20 deathbell, 20 nightshade and 20 nirnroot. Am I sensing that you may be interested in gathering these rare ingredients for me?"*
Answer in the affirmative.
Ingun will be pleased: *"That means more time for my experiments and less time in the field. Much appreciated."*

### Notable Harvest Locations

Ingun needs you to hunt down 20 Deathbells, 20 Nirnroot, and 20 Nightshade.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") | Grows in the salt marshes of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") and [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), including a number of specimens in both [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Planted specimens can be found in the [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") and [Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack") gardens, as well as [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze") in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"). They also grow near each city's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead") or graveyard. Finally, you can cultivate this plant, if you have a garden or farm. |
| [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") | Grows near water anywhere. You can collect 9 samples from [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"), which is close to Riften. See [the Nirnroot distribution map](/wiki/File:SR-Skyrim-Map-Nirnroot.png "File:SR-Skyrim-Map-Nirnroot.png") to find the closest samples. |
| [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") | Grows in places of death. Check the cemeteries at [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Also check [Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest") and outside the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") west of Falkreath. Finally, you can cultivate this plant, if you have a garden or farm. |

### Reward

Ingun will reward you with leveled amount of gold (listed in the table below) for each set of ingredients brought to her.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

After you have delivered and been paid for all three samples, it will behoove you to see what else you can procure from her. Hint to her: "That was the last of the ingredients."
To which she will reply: *"Yes, Master Elgrim will be pleased I've restored his stock of these rare ingredients. I feel I owe a bit more than some meaningless coin for all your diligence. Here, this key unlocks my supply chest at Elgrim's Elixirs. Feel free to take what you need from time to time. I'll be refilling it once every few days or so."*
The chest is found in the back of Elgrim's Elixirs, and she will restock it with 2 - 5 random leveled potions every few days. She will also remind you of this each time you exit conversation with her as she will say: *"Don't forget to check to check your supply chest from time to time."* The chest will require the key Ingun gave you each time it resets.

## Notes

- It is possible to give the items to [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") then quickly exit out of the conversation and enter the item menu then drop the items. The quest log will show "Find 20 <item name> for Ingun Black-Briar (0/20)". However as soon as Ingun is told "That was the last of the ingredients" the quest will update accordingly.
- You can use this quest to earn the [Hero of the People](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_the_People "Skyrim:Hero of the People") achievement quickly as every time you update your personal inventory from fewer than 20 to greater than or equal to 20 of any of the three ingredients, you will receive a quest objective update. You can therefore remain in a container menu and repeatedly shift these items back and forth in order to quickly unlock said achievement.

## Quest Stages

| Few and Far Between (FreeformRiften04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Find 20 nirnroot for Ingun Black-Briar (<Global=FFR04NirnCount>/20)  *Objective 20:* Find 20 nightshade for Ingun Black-Briar (<Global=FFR04NightshadeCount>/20)  *Objective 30:* Find 20 deathbell for Ingun Black-Briar (<Global=FFR04DeathbellCount>/20) |
|  |  | *(As you acquire 20 of each ingredient)* *Objective 15:* Bring the nirnroot to Ingun Black-Briar  *Objective 25:* Bring the nightshade to Ingun Black-Briar  *Objective 35:* Bring the deathbell to Ingun Black-Briar |
| 60 |  | *Objective 40:* Speak to Ingun Black-Briar |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 30, 40, 50, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften04`.

Fianna

**Fianna** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") who works as a maid in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

Fianna works alongside fellow servant [Gerda](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerda "Skyrim:Gerda") and they both spend the entire day sweeping the floor in the waiting area in front of the throne room. At 8am, Fianna starts sweeping the northwestern area, while Gerda sweeps the adjacent area. At 2pm they switch places and they both keep sweeping until 8pm when they head downstairs to their humble rooms in the [Jarl's quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Jarl%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Jarl's Quarters"). The entire night is spent either wandering, relaxing or eating, despite the presence of a bed nearby (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

Fianna wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). She also wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Dialogue

Fianna takes her job very seriously and even if you become a [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") she will remark:

:   *"Ain't nobody here high and mighty exceptin' the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") and don't you forget it!"*
:   *"Don't you go trackin' your dirty boots on my clean floor!"*
:   *"Soldiers! They're everywhere these days. And not a one of them knows how to pick up after themselves."*

## Bugs

- Fianna was supposed to sleep from 8pm to 8am, but her sleep package mistakenly includes other activities, causing her to stay up all night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), [Burguk's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse") | [Chief Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk") | "Any work to be done in the stronghold?" |  |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"), [Larak's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse") | [Chief Larak](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Larak "Skyrim:Chief Larak") | "Any work to be done in the stronghold?" | [Master Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") | [Uthgerd the Unbroken](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd_the_Unbroken "Skyrim:Uthgerd the Unbroken") | "You think you can take me on?" | [Marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"), [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades"), [Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |

[†](#note_benefit)Some of these benefits may be made available by other means.

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Speak to the quest giver.
2. Challenge them to a brawl.
3. Win the brawl.
4. Speak to them again.

## Detailed Walkthrough

If you talk to one of the quest givers they will eventually challenge you to a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl"). The dialogue and circumstances vary from person to person and are listed in the table above. Accepting the challenge means that you place a 100 gold bet on the outcome. You must then brawl them and win. Standard brawling rules apply and use of things such as hostile magic, shouts, and weapons will instantly change it from a brawl to a criminal assault.

Brawling should be relatively easy if you're wearing any armor and have gained at least a few levels. Only low level players on higher difficulties may have issues with winning a brawl. If you are having problems, use some potions and spells with lingering effects and don't forget about racial powers. It may be of use as well to read more in-depth information on [unarmed combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat#Unarmed_Combat "Skyrim:Combat"). You do not gain any experience from the unarmed combat during a brawl, although you may gain experience in armor skills.

You can only win a brawl with any given person once. If you lose the brawl, you will not get your wagered money back, although you will be able to get a rematch. If you win the brawl, you will get your wager back and receive an additional 100 gold.

## Notes

- There are other quests that simply involve brawling such as [Bloody Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Nose "Skyrim:Bloody Nose") that are in fact separate from this quest, despite being nearly identical in nature.
- When you engage in a brawl, viewing NPCs become immersed and tend to run around the fight. This can be quite annoying, as they can potentially run between you and your combatant which can lead you to accidentally punching one of the excited onlookers, which counts as an assault. Also, if you run away from the fight and exit through any doors, the first four NPCs who witness your fight will keep following you and will still think you are in a brawl until you fast travel.
- Certain considerations apply to the brawl itself:
  - Although your opponent may say "No magic," you can in fact use magic on yourself, such as [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)"), [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health"), or [ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward_(spells) "Skyrim:Ward (spells)") spells. However, using spells on your opponent, even beneficial healing spells, will count as assault.
  - Wearing the [Ebony Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Mail "Skyrim:Ebony Mail") or using a cloaking spell will also count as assault. However, wearing [Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Armor_of_Retribution "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Armor of Retribution")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") does not.
  - You can use a shield bash to "punch" your opponent.
- Winning the brawl will raise the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of the challenger. This will allow you to take low-value items they own, and they may become available as [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") or potential [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") partners. See the individual NPC pages for details.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold (with the exception of quest givers who live in Orc strongholds).
- Only one radiant quest of a similar type can be assigned at any given time. However, the dialogue to start the brawl is part of the quest, and the quest starts silently when you approach a location containing a quest giver. If two quest givers are near each other (e.g., Cosnach and Chief Burguk), the quest may start for one and block the dialogue to brawl with the other. Besides winning the brawl, the quest will also silently stop after some time away from the location.

## Bugs

- Sometimes your opponent may draw their weapon and attack you like in a normal fight. In this case, your only options are to yield or kill them (except Rolff, who is essential), and it is unlikely you will be able to properly complete the quest even if you try again. **?**
- Having the [Fists of Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Fists_of_Steel "Skyrim:Fists of Steel") perk may cause your opponent to remain in bleedout mode after you win the fight. Unequipping your Heavy Armor gauntlets will resolve this. **?**
- Engaging in a brawl for this quest can cause the [Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal") to permanently lose its ability to detect life and trigger guard hostility. **?**

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor017 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor017`.

# Skyrim:Fihada

## Overview

| Fihada (RefID: 000198B1) | | | |

Fihada

**Fihada** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [fletcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Fletcher_(class) "Skyrim:Fletcher (class)") and the owner of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") shop similarly named [Fletcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Fletcher_(place) "Skyrim:Fletcher (place)") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

His room is located above the main trading room and he sleeps there every night between midnight and 8am. He then unlocks the store and spends the next ten hours standing behind the counter, offering his wares to customers. At 6pm he will keep the shop open but will wander around, at times cooking or eating. At 8pm he heads down to the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") for a meal and some socializing with the other citizens. He stays there until his bedtime at midnight.

He wears a regular set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d8 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0003452f "Skyrim:Boots") and carries his [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") with 15 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"). He also carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), the [store key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Solitude_Fletcher "Skyrim:Key to Solitude Fletcher") and a variety of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When you enter his shop, he will bid you welcome, with a spontaneous:

:   *"Your path has brought you to the finest fletcher in all the land."*

His normal greetings:

:   *"Hello and welcome, my friend. How may I help you on this fine day?"*
:   *"True, I may look the part of dashing swordsman, but I prefer the art of wit to that of warfare."*
:   *"Your typical Solitude wench is like the city itself. Stormy exterior, but ah the charms that lie within..."*
:   *"A sharp mind beats a sharp blade any day. Words to live by."*

:   **I need some arrows that can take down a dragon...**
:   *"Why of course. And will you also be needing the bow that shoots rainbows? Or perhaps a quiver that dispenses beer? Look, if you want arrows we have them, but don't insult my intelligence."*

After doing business with him, he may close the conversation with:

:   *"Perhaps I'll be seeing more of you."*
:   *"Please come back if you're ever in need of fletching supplies."*

### Conversations

Inside the fletcher, Fihada will occasionally have conversations with his apprentice, [Jawanan](/wiki/Skyrim:Jawanan "Skyrim:Jawanan"):

:   **Fihada**: *"How's it coming there, Jawanan?"*
:   **Jawanan**: *"Slow, but looking good, sir."*
:   **Fihada**: *"Slow's the only way to do it! Work too hard and you'll warp the wood."*

:   **Jawanan**: *"Fihada, where did you learn how to make bows so well?"*
:   **Fihada**: *"The same place I learned my charm and quick wits: I used to be an Imperial ranger, my boy!"*
:   **Jawanan**: *"Wish I could learn some of that charm. I'm just good with bows, not people."*
:   **Fihada**: *"You'd make a better Imperial ranger than me. I may have charmed the locals, but my fellow soldiers hated my waggling tongue."*

When visiting the inn in the evenings, he will often turn to the female guests and make them an offer:

:   **Fihada:** *"Can I buy you a drink, darling?"*
:   **[Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis"):** *"Oh, yes please!"* or *"You can buy me whatever you want!"*

## Rumors

His apprentice, Jawanan, will refer you to him if spoken to:

:   *"If you're looking for any archery or fletching supplies, you should see Fihada. I'm just the apprentice."*

While Fihada seems generally popular around town, there is one person that doesn't seem to be impressed by his act: [Odar](/wiki/Skyrim:Odar "Skyrim:Odar"), the cook at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). When he visits the courtyard of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"), he can be observed talking to Jawanan about him:

:   **Odar**: *"How do you put up with that fop Fihada?"*
:   **Jawanan**: *"I once saw Fihada put an arrow in between the eyes of a [Blackblood Marauder](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") at five hundred paces. You don't put up with a man like that. He puts up with you."*

## Unused Dialogue

Based on an unused line of dialogue, it appears that Fihada was originally meant to comment on your loudness when entering the store. At which point you could mention it to him:

:   **I didn't make that much noise.**
:   *"Please. You're in the presence of a born huntsman. I can hear the sweat sliding down your forehead."*

As is the case with *many* Solitude citizens, you can find a lot of earlier versions of Fihada's dialogue still present in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"):

| Final | Early |
| --- | --- |
| *"True, I may look the part of dashing swordsman, but I prefer the art of wit to that of warfare."* | *"I realize you may mistake me for a dashing swordsman, but I prefer the art of wit to that of warfare."* |
| *"Your typical Solitude wench is like the city itself. Stormy exterior, but ah the charms that lie within..."* | *"A piece of advice... do not underestimate the beauty of Solitude's fair ladies. Like the city itself, they hide their charms behind stormy exteriors!"* |
| *"Perhaps I'll be seeing more of you."* | *"I hope I'll see you around then."* |
| *"Please come back if you're ever in need of fletching supplies."* | *"Come back for any of your fletching needs."* |
| **I need some arrows that can take down a dragon...** *"Why of course. And will you also be needing the bow that shoots rainbows? Or perhaps a quiver that dispenses beer? Look, if you want arrows we have them, but don't insult my intelligence."* | **I need some arrows to take down dragons.** *"And I could use a bow that shot lightning and a gold chamber pot to piss in. If you want arrows we have them, but if I wanted to hunt dragons I would use shouts, not a bow."* |

In the DialogueViews files, you can even find an earlier version of his unused dialogue as seen above. The first two sentences are also noted in the Creation Kit, but the other two are only found in the former files:

:   *"Please. You have stepped into the realm of a hunter. A person who breathes only with the wind itself. Your clamorous steps ring like a thousand men treading across a thousand battlefields. They volume alone hurts my trained ears."*

## Notes

- If Fihada dies, Jawanan will take over running the store, offering the same merchant services as Fihada.
- Fihada has relationship markers set up which show that he is friends with [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand"), [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund"), and even [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"). None of these people will ever address him or mention any kind of relation with him, however.

## Bugs

- Fihada cannot make use of the fletcher-specific merchant dialogue because he is not a part of the `JobFletcherFaction`, which is required for it to play.

# Skyrim:Fijeh

## Overview

| Fijeh (RefID: FE[xxx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID#Creation_Club "Skyrim:Form ID")826) | | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [ccEDHSSE003\_RedguardEliteFaction](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:CcEDHSSE003_RedguardEliteFaction&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:CcEDHSSE003 RedguardEliteFaction (page does not exist)") | | |

Fijeh

**Fijeh** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [Alik'r](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior") and leader of the [Remnants](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Remnants&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Remnants (page does not exist)"). He has been monitoring you for some time and seeks your help in rescuing his comrade [Rakeed](/wiki/Skyrim:Rakeed "Skyrim:Rakeed") from [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") custody.

## Related Quests

- **[Interception](/wiki/Skyrim:Interception "Skyrim:Interception")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments"): Aid the Hammerfell resistance.

## Quest-Related Events

After receiving his [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Letter_to_(Player) "Skyrim:Fijeh's Letter to (Player)") and travelling to [Purewater Run](/wiki/Skyrim:Purewater_Run "Skyrim:Purewater Run"), Fijeh will be waiting for you next to a small waterfall:

:   **You must be Fijeh.**
:   *"Correct."*

:   :   **I'd like to help find your missing Remnant, Rakeed. What comes next?**

:   :   **Actually, I don't have time to deal with this right now.**
    :   *"Unfortunate, but someone else will take care of it."*

:   :   **I don't work for free. Before this goes further, we need to talk about payment.**
    :   *"A little coin always greases the wheels."*
    :   *"How much?"*

| Option | Dialogue | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 400 gold seems reasonable. | *"For that price? Sure."* | | | |
| I wouldn't do this for any less than 800 gold.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"How can I argue with that?"* **Failed**: *"Nah, I don't think so."* | | | |
| There's other contracts I could be working right now. 1600 gold.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"How can I argue with that?"* **Failed**: *"You expect me to believe that?"* | | | |

After agreeing on a price, the conversation returns to the mission:

:   **It's settled then. What's next?**

Alternatively, if you left the dialogue after agreeing on payment:

:   **Now that we've agreed on payment, what's the next step?**

Either way, the conversation continues if the task is accepted:

:   *"It's all in [this note](/wiki/Skyrim:Fijeh%27s_Instructions "Skyrim:Fijeh's Instructions")."*
:   *"Now... this conversation never happened. Understood?"*

    :   **I'll return soon.**
    :   *"Good luck out there."*
    :   **I hope Rakeed is worth all of this trouble.**
    :   *"Good luck out there."*

After collecting intel from the [two](/wiki/Skyrim:Josla "Skyrim:Josla") [spies](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirayar "Skyrim:Sirayar"), return to Fijeh to report the findings:

:   **[Ismal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ismal "Skyrim:Ismal") has been traveling with a caravan of Thalmor to Morrowind.**
:   *"You've done well."*

    :   **They will enter Skyrim from the southwest, passing by [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge").**
    :   *"It just so happens, I've got some scouts along the road. Meet up with them, and together see if you can't overpower the caravan."*

        :   **Sounds good.**
        :   **I prefer to work alone.**
        :   *"I understand."*
        :   *"Go in quiet, break our man out, then get out of there. Don't risk combat if you can avoid it. If you can't, then give 'em hell."*

Whether you choose to go in alone or with the scouts, the conversation continues:

:   *"Here, [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Remnant_Supply_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Keys") is for you."*

    :   **I'll make sure your man gets out safely.**
    :   *"Stay sharp out there."*
    :   **I only want to kill Thalmor. I can't promise anything else.**
    :   *"It can't be helped."*
    :   *"Stay sharp out there."*

Upon returning to the cavern with Rakeed, Fijeh will he impressed and happy to see you:

:   *"You made it! I'm impressed. It was a gamble, but turned out well."*
:   **Good luck out there. I hope we meet again someday.**
:   **More than deserving of some payment, I'd say.**

Whichever way you reply, Fijeh's response will be the same.

:   *"Thank you. Here, this is for you."*
:   *"May the gods keep you."*

Fijeh's reward will be 400 [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") unless he was previously persuaded to supply more. After saying goodbye, both he and Rakeed will turn invisible and disappear from the game.
