# Skyrim:Filial Bonds

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood")'s brother, [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild"), who may have become a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), and [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill increase |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood")) |
| ID: | DLC2WB01 |

Torkild transforming into a werebear

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood").
2. Randomly locate Wulf's brother [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild").
3. Defeat Torkild when he is a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear").
4. Examine Torkild's body.
5. Return to Wulf.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Talk to [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). He will ask you to find his brother, [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild"). Torkild will appear randomly while wandering Solstheim. While speaking with him, he will turn into a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear") and you will be forced to kill him. Afterward, search his body and take the [letter to Wulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild%27s_Letter_to_Wulf "Skyrim:Torkild's Letter to Wulf") from him.

Return to Wulf Wild-Blood in Skaal Village and give him the letter. He will thank you, and give you a one point skill boost to several [combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") skills: [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), and [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed").

## Notes

- If you cannot find Torkild, there are eight places where he can appear. The one near Glacial Cave is probably the best choice, since the spawn point is close to the cave and you can fast travel there every so often and re-check.

| More Likely | Less Likely |
| --- | --- |
| - The area at the base of the waterfall west of [Glacial Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Cave "Skyrim:Glacial Cave"). - The plateau between [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") and [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave"). - A section of path about half-way between [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") and [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal"). | - The shoreline west of [Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine"). - Where you find Haknir's treasure, south of [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave"). - On the point southeast of [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat")/due north of [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak"). - Just north of Raven Rock, northeast of where the path up from the mine lets out. - On the mainland northwest of [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal"). |

- One possible circuit to check all eight places:

:   :   Fast travel to Glacial Cave, and walk west to check the waterfall.
    :   Fast travel to Bristleback Cave. Walk north and uphill to check the plateau.
    :   Walk back south to the shoreline, and continue south along the shore to check the area near the chest with Haknir's treasure.
    :   Walk south along the shore, past the big waterfall with all the netch, to check the shore west of Damphall Mine.

        :   Sometimes the NPCs here will spawn right at the waterline and then walk west into the ocean.
    :   Fast travel to Nchardak, and then walk north to check the point north of Nchardak.
    :   Fast travel to Haknir's Shoal. Swim west to the mainland shore, then walk north along the shore to check that area.
    :   Walk back south along the shore, until just north of the waterfall. Walk southwest, uphill, until you reach the path to Benkongerike, then turn and walk northwest to check that area.
    :   Fast travel to Raven Rock and head for Raven Rock Mine. At the smelter, turn and walk east, uphill, and check that area.

- While the quest [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha") is active, you cannot give the letter to Wulf.
- If you enter werewolf form to fight Torkild and choose to feed on him, you may temporarily be unable to search him. If you wait or fast travel elsewhere, you should be able to obtain the letter.

## Bugs

- It is possible Torkild will already be dead upon finding him (e.g. something else killed him before you were able to talk to him). This should not cause any problems with the quest, as you can still take the letter off his body. When talking with Wulf afterward the dialogue will still be about him turning into a werebear and you having to kill him.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The letter to Wulf may be removed from your inventory prematurely. This will not affect the quest.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2WB01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2WB01`.

Filnjar's House

**Filnjar's House** is a house in the small mining settlement of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").

It is the residence of town [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar"). It consists of one area only, *[Filnjar's House](#Filnjar.27s_House)*.

As is custom with the houses of blacksmiths, all tools are located on the porch outside the house.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") |

## Filnjar's House

The interior of Filnjar's House

The house consists of a ground floor and a basement, the latter used mostly for storage. The front door opens to the sight of a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") leaning against the fireplace, a small table with two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a copy of *[The Cabin in the Woods](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cabin_in_the_Woods "Skyrim:The Cabin in the Woods")*. Next to the table is Filnjar's owned bed with a minor loot chest and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#Shoes "Skyrim:Clothing") on the floor. In the southwestern corner sits a clothes wardrobe with a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") on top, along with a small table that holds five gold coins, a coin purse and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Lastly, a food barrel stands in the adjacent corner.

To the left of the entrance stands a table with a variety of food and drinks; one bunch of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), one bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and one of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two bottles of [nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). The shelves next to the table hold even more food, two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a cluster of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). Hanging above the shelves are three [dried elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and one sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Finishing off the area is a food barrel in the northeastern corner, right above the stairs leading down to the basement.

The basement is spacious but pretty barebones. A food barrel stands at the foot of the stairs, next to a table with a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). Adjacent to this table is another table with a single loaf of bread. In the western part of the room, past the hay piles, is a food barrel, a wardrobe with clothes, and an unlocked chest with some random gold and minor loot. More loot can be gathered from an end table that has two [blacksmith's potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion") on top.

Filnjar

**Filnjar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") that lives in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). He spends most of his day working at his forge before going to bed at midnight. He can be bartered with and has a base amount of 500 gold. He sells various [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") items, [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), and [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). He acts as the town's unofficial leader and enlists you to clear the [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") that have recently infested it. He has great faith in the mine and believes there is more to be discovered than what they've tapped into thus far. Upon raising Filnjar's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"), he will become a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

He wears a typical red [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron#0005b69f "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b69e "Skyrim:Shoes"). He carries a leveled mace (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Filnjar%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Filnjar's House") to his house, and a [selection of common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Filnjar starts off his day at 6am and spends an hour resting in [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar%27s_House "Skyrim:Filnjar's House"). At 7am, he goes outside to his porch to work on the forge for most of the day. After twelve hours of working, he finally stops and heads back inside his house to consume his dinner for an hour. At 8pm, he sits around the campfire in the middle of town for four hours. At midnight, he heads back home for six hours of sleep, and repeats his schedule the following day.

## Related Quests

- **[Mine or Yours](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_or_Yours "Skyrim:Mine or Yours")**: Help Filnjar by ridding the [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
- **[Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences")**: Retrieve an [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quest Items") sample from Filnjar.
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Dialogue

When greeted he will talk about his small town:

:   *"If you're looking for supplies, I'd advise heading to Riften."*
:   *"What brings you out to Shor's Stone?"*
:   *"The mine will be running better than ever thanks to you."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **Tell me about the mine.**
:   *"Redbelly Mine gets its name from the red mist filling the place. You get used to it after a while... kind of smells like the hot springs out in the tundra. No idea what's causing it though."*

When exiting conversation, he'll say:

:   *"Don't kid yourself... stone runs in our blood."*

### Truth Ore Consequences

During [Truth Ore Consequences](/wiki/Skyrim:Truth_Ore_Consequences "Skyrim:Truth Ore Consequences"), [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") will tell you to pick up an ore sample from Filnjar and return it to her. When you tell Filnjar you are here for the ore sample:

:   **I'm here for Elgrim's ore sample.**
:   *"It's about time; I sent them a letter weeks ago. That [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")... he'd forget his own pants if his wife didn't help him dress. Here you go. Tell Hafjorg that she can chip off whatever she thinks is a fair trade for their time."*
:   **What's so special about this ore?**
:   *"Redbelly is supposed to be nothing but an iron mine. Been working it for years. Then right before the spiders had moved in, we found that chunk of ore. Never seen anything like it. I want to know what I'm dealing with before I start tearing it out of the ground."*

### Mine or Yours

When you first meet him, he will grumble about the sorry state of the mine:

:   *"I hope you haven't arrived here looking for work in the mine."*
:   *"Sorry, the mine's dry right now."*
:   *"I hate seeing a good mine go to waste like that, you know?"*

When asked about what is wrong with the mine:

:   **What's wrong with the mine?**
:   *"It's full of spiders, that's what's wrong with it! Almost killed [Grogmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag") and me when they showed up. I'm worried that they'll come out of the mine looking for food soon... then we're in even bigger trouble."*
:   **The town guards can't help you?**
:   *"They're as useless as a fifth wheel on a wagon. Gave me some sort of a line about "keeping an eye out for enemy soldiers." What's the point in protecting this place if the mine's completely useless? Idiots."*

:   :   **I'm going to pass on that.**
    :   *"I never asked you to help in the first place. Why would I? Everyone in Skyrim only helps themselves."*

:   :   **I'll clear them out for you.**
    :   *"Tell you what. Keep to your word, and I'll line your pockets with as much as I can scrape up."*

If you ask about the spiders infesting the mine, he'll tell you:

:   **Tell me about the spiders infesting the mine.**
:   *"Moved right in and made themselves at home. Did it overnight. I'm not even sure exactly where they came from. No one's been hurt yet, and they seem to be staying in the mine, but who knows how long that will last? If we can't get back into the mine, our town is sunk."*

As you are leaving for the mine, he will express concerns for your life with the remark:

:   *"I don't want to be responsible for sending you to your death. Be careful in the mine."*

If you greet him before you kill the spiders, he'll comment:

:   *"The spiders put you through the ringer*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*?"*
:   *"Nasty little buggers, aren't they?"*

After you have cleaned out the mine:

:   **I've cleared the mine of spiders.**
:   *"Gone? Every one of them? Why, that's incredible."*

If you cleared the mine before talking to him about the spider infestation, you can notify him that you already cleared the mine:

:   **I've already cleared Redbelly Mine.**
:   *"Wait... you mean you killed every last one of them? I can't believe it!"*

Either way, he'll then say:

:   *"Finally, we can reopen the mine and put Shor's Stone back on the map! Here, please accept this gift as a token of our gratitude."*

## Conversations

At night, he can be seen conversing with other Shor's Stone residents:

**[Odfel](/wiki/Skyrim:Odfel "Skyrim:Odfel")**: *"You think living with Grogmar is easy? Did you see how he lives?"*
**Filnjar**: *"You two will just have to learn to get along until we can build you another house."*
**Odfel**: *"At this rate that'll never happen."*
**Filnjar**: *"Quit your bellyaching. We've all got our problems."*

**Grogmar**: *"I've been cracking rock ever since I was able to hold a pickaxe and I'm telling you, this mine is drying up."*
**Filnjar**: *"And I'm telling you, you're wrong."*
**Grogmar**: *"What makes you so sure? What if I'm right?"*
**Filnjar**: *"I know there's ore still in there, I can smell it. If you think you're right then you can pack up and leave any time you like."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Filnjar's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of heavy armor (unmatched, unenchanted; Ebony is best possible) |  |
| 1 | Complete leveled set of light armor (unmatched, unenchanted; Glass is best possible) |  |

## Notes

- Filnjar may be killed by the local wildlife or the spiders from Redbelly Mine.
- There's an unused conversation present for Filnjar and [Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka"), the marketplace vendor in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). However, as Grelka and Filnjar never meet, this conversation doesn't ever play. Evidently, [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja")'s role originally belonged to Grelka.

:   **Filnjar**: *"How are your parents faring, Grelka? Doing better than we are I would guess."*
:   **Grelka**: *"It's no feast in their neck of the woods either. Last time I was up there, father said they were barely scraping by."*
:   **Filnjar**: *"This [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") is taking its toll on all of us. Miners are some of the hardest hit."*
:   **Grelka**: *"That's what scares me. I'm afraid I'll travel to [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") and find it burned to the ground."*

## Bugs

- You cannot invest with Filnjar through the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. He can now be invested with like other shopkeepers.

# Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, checked by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **The [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") are after [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn"). Help him get to safety.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| Reward: | [Leveled gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | MQ201Malborn |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") | | |

Malborn is down on his luck

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") after the quest [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity").
2. Locate the [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit").
3. Speak to [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad").
4. Kill the assassin.
5. Return to Malborn.

### An Old Friend

If you manage to get [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") out of the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") alive during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), after the end of that quest, he will run all the way to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") seeking shelter in the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub"), a [Dunmer](/wiki/Lore:Dunmer "Lore:Dunmer") tavern located in the Gray Quarter. If you used [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas") as a distraction during that quest, she will be nearby (see [Bugs](#Bugs)). Upon your next visit anywhere near the city of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") a hidden timer of 1 in-game day starts, so be sure to receive and complete this quest fast. Approaching Malborn in the New Gnisis Corneclub will have him explain his situation: due to his treachery, he is obviously blacklisted by the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") so he has decided to flee to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"); however, every time he tries to sneak out of Windhelm, he sees a suspicious [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") outside the gates. Convinced that the Thalmor have sent an assassin to kill him, and still blaming you and [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") for putting him in a tight spot, the scared Malborn is now stuck in the Cornerclub and will request your assistance to get him to safety.

An assassin waits for his prey outside Windhelm

### A Stranger in Their Midst

Malborn will not provide a description of the alleged Khajiit assassin, saying only that he is standing outside the city gates. Your map marker will disappear when you exit Windhelm, so cross the bridge and make your way to the [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") where [Ma'dran's Khajiit caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders#Ma.27dran.27s_Caravan "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") usually camps (it may or may not be there, depending on its schedule). If the hidden timer hasn't run out yet, instead of Ma'dran's group, [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad") and [his caravan members](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders#Ri.27saad.27s_Caravan "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") will be there, way off course from their usual route. In any case there will always be at least one Khajiit named [J'datharr](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27datharr "Skyrim:J'datharr") present, who stands apart from any others.

To unmask the real assassin, speak to the caravan Khajiits. A specific dialogue cue will appear when you speak to Ri'saad:

:   **I'm looking for a Khajiit... might be a Thalmor spy.**

    :   *"Ah. You must mean that one over there. He's not one of us. Thalmor filth, eh? Giving all Khajiit a bad name."*

Doing so will allow you to confront the stranger in dialogue. When approached, J'datharr will initially try to brush you off, but upon hearing that you have a message from Malborn, he'll reply with: *"Malborn? Ah... very good. I think we understand each other"* and become hostile. The Khajiiti caravanners will not intervene on either side, so it's a simple duel to the death. After the fight, you can loot his body to find [J'datharr's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27datharr%27s_Note "Skyrim:J'datharr's Note"), obviously written by the Thalmor. Lastly, return to New Gnisis Cornerclub to tell Malborn the good news. He will be grateful and reward you with some of the gold he stole from the Thalmor. He will then leave Windhelm, running towards the safety of Morrowind; after passing [Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest"), he disappears from the game and the quest will be complete. If Brelas was at the Cornerclub with him, she will also flee to Morrowind and disappear from the game.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21+ | 250 |

## Notes

- If you used [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas") as a distraction during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), whether or not you freed her from the dungeon, she will join Malborn in Windhelm (see [Bugs](#Bugs)), and also accompany him to Morrowind. However, no-one will acknowledge her presence, nor will she gain any new dialogue.
- After freeing Malborn during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), Ri'saad and his caravan will move near [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"). They resume their usual schedule when the hidden timer runs out or when the assassin is dead.
- The 1 in-game day timer is triggered by the player arriving anywhere near Windhelm after Malborn flees during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity").
  -  To check the 1 in-game day timer you can use the console command `sqs MQ201Malborn`: if `Stage 110: 0` you still have time, if `Stage 110: 1` it has run-out.
- After killing the assassin, to avoid script conflict, it is safe to wait 24 in-game hours to make sure the hidden timer runs out before telling Malborn the assassin is dead.
- Immediately after learning of the assassin's death, Malborn (and Brelas if present) leaves the city. He will run all the way to [Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest"), and get disabled from the game once reaching the podium with the [Decree of Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Decree_of_Monument "Skyrim:Decree of Monument").
  - As weak characters, they are high risk for dying from an animal or bandit attack on their run toward Morrowind. To prevent this, either accompany and defend them, or clear the animal and bandit attack spawn points along the route prior to informing Malborn that the assassin is dealt with. Waiting/fast traveling also lets the game safely disable them.
- If Malborn dies (even after receiving the reward) before he is disabled, the quest will fail.
- According to the Creation Kit, there was supposed to be a way for you to betray Malborn by telling him there was no assassin, letting him believe it was safe for him to flee to Morrowind only to find his killer waiting for him just outside the city's stables. This option didn't make it to the final version of the game.

## Bugs

- If you freed Brelas from the Thalmor Embassy Dungeon during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), after arriving in Windhelm she runs over to the left of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") and vanishes, rather than going to [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If you miss speaking to Ri'saad before the 1 in-game day timer runs out, he will return to his usual route and the final dialogue with the assassin cannot be unlocked, preventing the quest from progressing.
  - If you manage to move Ri'saad near [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") (for example by making him follow you, casting a [frenzy spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect)#Spells "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") on him and [pacifying](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(effect) "Skyrim:Pacify (effect)") him afterwards) his dialogue option will reappear.
  - Killing J'datharr will advance the quest. If you don't want to just attack him in cold blood, cast a [frenzy spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect)#Spells "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") on him; even if his level is too high to be affected, he will turn hostile, allowing you to kill him and continue the quest. This skips two Stages but won't cause any script conflict.
  -  The console command `setstage MQ201Malborn 30` will place a quest marker on the assassin and allow you to talk to him. After picking *"Malborn has a message for you."* he will turn hostile and you can kill him normally.
- J'datharr carries a nameless object. When dropped, it turns into a large red square with a pink exclamation mark inside it and cannot be picked back up. This is due to the item lacking a world model; the item is actually a world item internally known as `HelgenCandleLight01NS`, a light source to be specific. It is unknown why he possesses this, but it could be due to him needing a light source for his torch holding animation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=274)) He now has a normal torch item in its stead.
-  If you have the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") installed, it moves dialogue from Ri'saad to [Ma'dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27dran "Skyrim:Ma'dran") (and related [caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders")). This change is not listed in [USLEEP's changelog](https://www.afkmods.com/Unofficial%20Skyrim%20Legendary%20Edition%20Patch%20Version%20History.html) nor in [USSEP's changelog](https://www.afkmods.com/Unofficial%20Skyrim%20Special%20Edition%20Patch%20Version%20History.html). **?**[*verification needed — does it happen with USLEEP too? (see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin#It_is_always_Ri.27saad))*]

## Quest Stages

| Find the Thalmor Assassin (MQ201Malborn) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | I met Malborn hiding out in Windhelm. He thinks there's a Thalmor assassin on his trail, a Khajiit, waiting for him outside the city. I promised I'd take care of this assassin, if there really is one. *Objective 10:* Find the Thalmor assassin |
| 100 |  | I met Malborn hiding out in Windhelm. I killed the Thalmor assassin who was on his trail. I should let him know it's safe for him to leave Windhelm. *Objective 20:* Tell Malborn the assassin is dead |
| 150 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 15, 30, 50, 80, 110, 200, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ201Malborn stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ201Malborn`.

# Skyrim:Finn's Lute

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the item, see [Finn's Lute (item)](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers") |
| Location(s): | [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave") |
| Reward: | +1 point to all [Stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skills |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers")) |
| ID: | BardsCollegeLute |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") | | |

Finn's Lute

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
2. Locate [Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") in [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave").
3. Return for your reward of a 1-point increase to all [Stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skills.

### A Unique Lute

Right after the Burning of [King Olaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") ends the quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), talking to the otherwise authoritarian [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers") will be somewhat wistful. When asked, she will tell you that a year ago, thieves broke into the College and stole her most precious item: the very first eight course lute ever created, namely [Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)"). As the Dean of Lute, Inge has been devastated ever since, but recently learned the location of the thieves, specifically [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), a cave in southeastern [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch").

### Stony Creek Cave

A small pond hides the entrance to the cave, complete with a dock and a boat. Upon entering, the sight of a waterfall and a dead Breton hanging from a tree trunk hints at things to come. Follow the only available path upstream and fight the expected [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") trying to protect their treasure. When the path splits in two, head right and beware of the [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap right before the chamber with the bandit leader. Pick the fight and search the body for *[Treasure Map X](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_X "Skyrim:Treasure Map X")*, then look around the area for interesting items, including a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, Part 4")*, an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), along with a few ingredients and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). Finally, open the chest and claim the lute and some valuable loot.

### An Unexpected Lesson

Before exiting the cave, it is possible to investigate the rest of the cave which will net you another fight against a bandit, along with a locked treasure chest, two [moonstone veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") and a waterfall hiding a shortcut from [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel"). Exit the mine the way you came and return to the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). Back at the College, Inge Six Fingers will be overwhelmed with joy. As she is unable to pay what the lute is worth, she will instead teach you a few tricks she has picked up over the years, and raise each of your [Stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skills by one point. This includes [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"), [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking"), [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), and [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech").

## Bugs

- After you turn in the quest, the lute will remain in your inventory, still marked as a quest item.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  -  You can remove the quest item using the Console and the following console code: `Player.removeitem 000DABAB 1`
- Finding the lute before the quest is assigned may result in the lute being stuck your inventory as a quest item even after finding Inge Six Fingers and telling her you have found it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- Finding the lute early may also result the quest objective becoming stuck in your journal, even after returning the lute and receiving your reward.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  - To resolve this, click on the "I've found Finn's Lute" option in dialogue when you speak to Inge, rather than the "Why are you sad?" option. It works out just as if you had accepted the quest and then found it.
  -  Alternatively, you can use the console code `setstage BardsCollegeLute 40` after accepting the quest, which will update it to telling you to give Inge the lute, allowing the quest to proceed as normal.

## Quest Stages

| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Give Finn's Lute to Inge |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BardsCollegeLute stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BardsCollegeLute`.

Finna

**Finna** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living at [Oslaf's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf%27s_House "Skyrim:Oslaf's House") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") with her husband [Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf") and their daughter [Aeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeta "Skyrim:Aeta"). She wears a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") and [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat"). She carries a [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Oslaf's House Key"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men")**: Travel to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") to learn the rest of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will").

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"I welcome you, friend of the Skaal."*
:   *"The dragons of old have returned! By the All-Maker, I hope they will leave our village alone."*
:   *"There is strength and courage in your eyes. You have the spirit of a great hunter."*
:   *"The [historian](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") has not stopped speaking your praises."*

### Conversations

Finna may be seen having some random conversations with her husband Oslaf:

:   **Oslaf**: *"There's a terrible ache in my back today."*
:   **Finna**: *"Complaining to me won't make your pain go away, Oslaf. Go and see Edla, perhaps she has a remedy."*
:   **Oslaf**: *"There's no time for that now, I have work to do."*
:   **Finna**: *"Then get back to it, you lazy horker! The day is wasting."*

:   **Oslaf**: *"Are the potatoes ready for eating? I want to roast them with some onions for the night's meal."*
:   **Finna**: *"Be patient, my husband. The crop doesn't grow faster because it hears your growling stomach."*
:   **Oslaf**: *"Hm, perhaps I'll make an offering to the All-Maker. He can make our potatoes ripen as surely as he makes the snow fall from the sky."*
:   **Finna**: *"I'm sure the All-Maker has more important concerns than your potatoes, Oslaf."*

### The Gardener of Men

If spoken to while Storn is reading the black book:

:   *"Storn! What is he doing?"*

After Storn dies, she approaches the corpse to pay her respects:

:   **Finna:** *"May the All-Maker guide your soul to the next life."*

If spoken to:

:   *"Storn was like a father to me. To all of us. I do not know what we will do without him."*
:   *"Leave us, please."*

# Skyrim:Fire Mage

## Overview

**Fire Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of fire mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level fire mages even at high levels, but boss-level fire mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Fire Mages

A Novice Fire Mage attacks with a blast of flame

Fire mages rely on their devastating fire-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, fire mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, fire mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers have the same gear as lower-level fire mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Fire Mage Bosses

Apprentice Fire Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level fire mages listed above. Fire Mage Adepts, Fire Mages, Fire Wizards and Pyromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers listed above, with the exception that Fire Mage Adepts and Fire Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts") rather than a Staff of Fireballs.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic fire mages that are Dark Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means fire mages are slightly more likely to be Dark Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Fire Mage

## Overview

**Fire Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of fire mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level fire mages even at high levels, but boss-level fire mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Fire Mages

A Novice Fire Mage attacks with a blast of flame

Fire mages rely on their devastating fire-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, fire mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, fire mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers have the same gear as lower-level fire mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Fire Mage Bosses

Apprentice Fire Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level fire mages listed above. Fire Mage Adepts, Fire Mages, Fire Wizards and Pyromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers listed above, with the exception that Fire Mage Adepts and Fire Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts") rather than a Staff of Fireballs.

## Named Fire Mages

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") | [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") | A representative of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") serving as an advisor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") | Wilderness | A pilgrim on her way to see the restored [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | The elemental mage leader of the mages found in the keep (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") | [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") | A hostile elemental mage living south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") | [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") | A Thalmor agent working for Ancano |
| [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") | [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") | A master wizard at the College of Winterhold, reporting directly to the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |
| [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked") | [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | An Altmer experimenting with magic on live subjects within the fort |
| [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") | [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | A Nord elemental mage performing sadistic experiments within the ruin |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic fire mages that are Dark Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means fire mages are slightly more likely to be Dark Elves than one of the other races.
